894 /************************************************************************
895  * name: odbc_set_cursor_name
896  * arguments:
897  * returns/side-effects:
898  * description:
899  * NOTE:
900  ************************************************************************/
901 PUBLIC RETCODE
902 odbc_set_cursor_name (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, char *cursor_name, short name_length)
903 {
904  if (cursor_name != NULL)
905  {
906  stmt->cursor = UT_MAKE_STRING (cursor_name, name_length);
907  }
908  return ODBC_SUCCESS;
909 }
910 
911 /************************************************************************
912  * name: odbc_get_cursor_name
913  * arguments:
914  * returns/side-effects:
915  * description:
916  * NOTE:
917  ************************************************************************/
918 PUBLIC RETCODE
919 odbc_get_cursor_name (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, SQLCHAR * cursor_name, SQLSMALLINT buffer_length, SQLLEN * name_length_ptr)
920 {
921  RETCODE rc, status = ODBC_SUCCESS;
922  char *pt;
923 
924  if (stmt->cursor != NULL)
925  {
926  pt = stmt->cursor;
927  }
928  else
929  {
930  pt = "";
931  }
932  rc = str_value_assign (pt, cursor_name, buffer_length, name_length_ptr);
933  if (rc == ODBC_SUCCESS_WITH_INFO)
934  {
935  odbc_set_diag (stmt->diag, "01004", 0, NULL);
936  status = rc;
937  }
938 
939  return status;
940 }
941 
942 
943 /************************************************************************
944 * name: odbc_bind_parameter
945 * arguments:
946 * returns/side-effects:
947 * description:
948 * NOTE:
949 * column_size에 대해서 고려하지 않고 있음.
950 ************************************************************************/
951 PUBLIC RETCODE
952 odbc_bind_parameter (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, SQLUSMALLINT parameter_num, SQLSMALLINT input_output_type,
953  SQLSMALLINT value_type, SQLSMALLINT parameter_type, SQLULEN column_size,
954  SQLSMALLINT decimal_digits, SQLPOINTER parameter_value_ptr, SQLLEN buffer_length,
955  SQLLEN * strlen_ind_ptr)
956 {
957  ODBC_DESC *apd = NULL, *ipd = NULL;
958  RETCODE rc;
959  short odbc_type;
960  long size;
961  ODBC_RECORD *record;
962 
963  apd = stmt->apd;
964  ipd = stmt->ipd;
965 
966 
967  /***** APD *****/
968  /* setting concise type */
969 
970  record = find_record_from_desc (apd, parameter_num);
971  if (record == NULL)
972  {
973  odbc_alloc_record (apd, NULL, parameter_num);
974  }
975 
976  if (value_type == SQL_C_DEFAULT)
977  {
978  value_type = default_type_to_c_type (value_type, parameter_type);
979  }
980 
981  rc = odbc_set_desc_field (apd, parameter_num, SQL_DESC_CONCISE_TYPE, (SQLPOINTER) value_type, 0, 1);
982  ERROR_GOTO (rc, error1);
983 
984  /* setting verbose type */
985  odbc_type = odbc_concise_to_verbose_type (value_type);
986 
987  rc = odbc_set_desc_field (apd, parameter_num, SQL_DESC_TYPE, (SQLPOINTER) odbc_type, 0, 1);
988  ERROR_GOTO (rc, error1);
989 
990  /* setting subcode type */
991  /* parameter type is c data type */
992  if (odbc_is_valid_c_interval_type (value_type) || odbc_is_valid_c_date_type (value_type))
993  {
994  odbc_type = odbc_subcode_type (value_type);
995  rc = odbc_set_desc_field (apd, parameter_num, SQL_DESC_DATETIME_INTERVAL_CODE, (SQLPOINTER) odbc_type, 0, 1);
996  ERROR_GOTO (rc, error1);
997  }
998 
999  /* char data type의 경우는 buffer_length를 octet_length로 사용한다. */
1000  size = odbc_octet_length (value_type, (int) buffer_length);
1001  rc = odbc_set_desc_field (apd, parameter_num, SQL_DESC_OCTET_LENGTH, (void *) size, 0, 1);
1002  ERROR_GOTO (rc, error1);
1003 
1004 
1005  rc = odbc_set_desc_field (apd, parameter_num, SQL_DESC_DATA_PTR, parameter_value_ptr, 0, 1);
1006  ERROR_GOTO (rc, error1);
1007 
1008  rc = odbc_set_desc_field (apd, parameter_num, SQL_DESC_OCTET_LENGTH_PTR, strlen_ind_ptr, 0, 1);
1009  ERROR_GOTO (rc, error1);
1010 
1011  rc = odbc_set_desc_field (apd, parameter_num, SQL_DESC_INDICATOR_PTR, strlen_ind_ptr, 0, 1);
1012  ERROR_GOTO (rc, error1);
1013 
1014  /***** IPD *****/
1015  record = find_record_from_desc (ipd, parameter_num);
1016  if (record == NULL)
1017  {
1018  odbc_alloc_record (ipd, NULL, parameter_num);
1019  }
1020  /* setting concise type */
1021  rc = odbc_set_desc_field (ipd, parameter_num, SQL_DESC_CONCISE_TYPE, (SQLPOINTER) parameter_type, 0, 1);
1022  ERROR_GOTO (rc, error2);
1023 
1024  /* setting verbose type */
1025  odbc_type = odbc_concise_to_verbose_type (parameter_type);
1026 
1027  rc = odbc_set_desc_field (ipd, parameter_num, SQL_DESC_TYPE, (SQLPOINTER) odbc_type, 0, 1);
1028  ERROR_GOTO (rc, error2);
1029 
1030  /* setting subcode type */
1031  /* parameter type is c data type */
1032  if (odbc_is_valid_c_interval_type (parameter_type) || odbc_is_valid_c_date_type (parameter_type))
1033  {
1034  odbc_type = odbc_subcode_type (parameter_type);
1035  rc = odbc_set_desc_field (ipd, parameter_num, SQL_DESC_DATETIME_INTERVAL_CODE, (SQLPOINTER) odbc_type, 0, 1);
1036  ERROR_GOTO (rc, error2);
1037  }
1038 
1039  if (parameter_type == SQL_CHAR || parameter_type == SQL_VARCHAR || parameter_type == SQL_LONGVARCHAR
1040  || parameter_type == SQL_BINARY || parameter_type == SQL_VARBINARY || parameter_type == SQL_LONGVARBINARY
1041  || odbc_is_valid_sql_date_type (parameter_type) || odbc_is_valid_sql_interval_type (parameter_type))
1042  {
1043 
1044  rc = odbc_set_desc_field (ipd, parameter_num, SQL_DESC_LENGTH, (SQLPOINTER) column_size, 0, 1);
1045  ERROR_GOTO (rc, error2);
1046  }
1047  else if (parameter_type == SQL_DECIMAL || parameter_type == SQL_NUMERIC || parameter_type == SQL_FLOAT
1048  || parameter_type == SQL_REAL || parameter_type == SQL_DOUBLE)
1049  {
1050 
1051  rc = odbc_set_desc_field (ipd, parameter_num, SQL_DESC_PRECISION, (SQLPOINTER) column_size, 0, 1);
1052  ERROR_GOTO (rc, error2);
1053  }
1054 
1055  if (parameter_type == SQL_TYPE_TIME || parameter_type == SQL_TIME || // for 2.x backward compatibility
1056  parameter_type == SQL_TYPE_TIMESTAMP || parameter_type == SQL_TIMESTAMP || // for 2.x backward
1057  // compatibility
1058  parameter_type == SQL_INTERVAL_SECOND || parameter_type == SQL_INTERVAL_DAY_TO_SECOND
1059  || parameter_type == SQL_INTERVAL_HOUR_TO_SECOND || parameter_type == SQL_INTERVAL_MINUTE_TO_SECOND)
1060  {
1061 
1062  rc = odbc_set_desc_field (ipd, parameter_num, SQL_DESC_PRECISION, (SQLPOINTER) decimal_digits, 0, 1);
1063  ERROR_GOTO (rc, error2);
1064  }
1065  else if (parameter_type == SQL_NUMERIC || parameter_type == SQL_DECIMAL)
1066  {
1067 
1068  rc = odbc_set_desc_field (ipd, parameter_num, SQL_DESC_SCALE, (SQLPOINTER) decimal_digits, 0, 1);
1069  ERROR_GOTO (rc, error2);
1070  }
1071 
1072  return ODBC_SUCCESS;
1073 
1074 error1:
1075  odbc_move_diag (stmt->diag, apd->diag);
1076  return ODBC_ERROR;
1077 
1078 error2:
1079  odbc_move_diag (stmt->diag, ipd->diag);
1080  return ODBC_ERROR;
1081 }
1082 
1083 /************************************************************************
1084 * name: odbc_num_params
1085 * arguments:
1086 * returns/side-effects:
1087 * description:
1088 * NOTE:
1089 * odbc_num_result_cols는 ird가 sql stmt에 맞게 생성되기 때문에
1090 * ird의 record개수가 num of result cols이지만,
1091 * odbc_num_params에서는 ipd가 자동적으로 생성되지 않기 때문에,
1092 * stmt->param_number의 member에 유지하고 있다.
1093 ************************************************************************/
1094 PUBLIC RETCODE
1095 odbc_num_params (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, short *parameter_count)
1096 {
1097 
1098  if (parameter_count)
1099  {
1100  *parameter_count = stmt->param_number;
1101  }
1102 
1103  return ODBC_SUCCESS;
1104 }
1105 
1106 /************************************************************************
1107 * name: odbc_prepare
1108 * arguments:
1109 * returns/side-effects:
1110 * description:
1111 * NOTE:
1112 * - statement_text가 null이면 DM error가 난다.
1113 * - IRD setting이 일어난다.
1114 * - Method에 의한 result set에 대해서
1115 * col type - SQL_VARCHAR
1116 * col precision - MAX_PRECISION을 적용하였다.
1117 ************************************************************************/
1118 PUBLIC RETCODE
1119 odbc_prepare (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, char *statement_text)
1120 {
1121  int cci_rc;
1122  T_CCI_ERROR cci_err_buf;
1123  T_CCI_COL_INFO *cci_col_info;
1124  int column_number;
1125  char flag_cci_prepare;
1126 
1127  // init & reset
1128  // reset - result set and related info, sql statement
1129  if (stmt->stmthd > 0)
1130  {
1131  cci_close_req_handle (stmt->stmthd);
1132  stmt->stmthd = -1;
1133  }
1134  reset_result_set (stmt);
1135  reset_descriptor (stmt->ird);
1136  stmt->param_number = 0;
1137 
1138  reset_revised_sql (stmt);
1139  NA_FREE (stmt->sql_text);
1140 
1141  stmt->sql_text = UT_MAKE_STRING (statement_text, -1);
1142  stmt->revised_sql.sql_text = UT_MAKE_STRING (statement_text, -1);
1143  // revise sql text because oid string value
1144  stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_num =
1145  replace_oid (stmt->revised_sql.sql_text, &stmt->revised_sql.org_param_pos, &stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_pos,
1146  &stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_val);
1147 
1148  flag_cci_prepare = get_flag_of_cci_prepare (stmt);
1149  cci_rc = cci_prepare (stmt->conn->connhd, stmt->revised_sql.sql_text, flag_cci_prepare, &cci_err_buf);
1150  if (cci_rc < 0)
1151  goto error;
1152 
1153  stmt->stmthd = cci_rc;
1154 
1155  // set fetch size
1156  if (stmt->conn->fetch_size > 0)
1157  {
1158  cci_fetch_size (stmt->stmthd, stmt->conn->fetch_size);
1159  }
1160 
1161  // get param number
1162  stmt->param_number = cci_get_bind_num (stmt->stmthd) - stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_num;
1163 
1164  // second argument is stmt->stmt_type
1165  cci_col_info = cci_get_result_info (stmt->stmthd, &stmt->stmt_type, &column_number);
1166 
1167  // check read-only mode
1168  if (stmt->conn->attr_access_mode == SQL_MODE_READ_ONLY && !RESULTSET_STMT_TYPE (stmt->stmt_type))
1169  {
1170  odbc_set_diag (stmt->diag, "HY000", 0, "SQL Mode is read-only.");
1171  return ODBC_ERROR;
1172  }
1173 
1174  create_ird (stmt, cci_col_info, column_number);
1175 
1176  return ODBC_SUCCESS;
1177 
1178 error:
1179  odbc_set_diag_by_cci (stmt->diag, cci_rc, &cci_err_buf);
1180  return ODBC_ERROR;
1181 }
1182 
1183 /************************************************************************
1184 * name: odbc_execute
1185 * arguments:
1186 * returns/side-effects:
1187 * description:
1188 * NOTE:
1189 * 1) 현재 array parameter bind & execution을 지원하고 있지 않다.
1190 * 2) error가 발생한 경우, SQL_ERROR나 SQL_SUCCESS_WITH_INFO를 return한다.
1191 * 이 때는 autocommit mode일지라도 autocommit은 일어나지 않는다.(rollback도 없다.)
1192 ************************************************************************/
1193 PUBLIC RETCODE
1194 odbc_execute (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt)
1195 {
1196  short count, valid_param_count;
1197  short sql_type;
1198  T_CCI_A_TYPE a_type;
1199  T_CCI_U_TYPE u_type;
1200  void *c_value = NULL, *sql_value = NULL;
1201  short is_data_at_exec = 0;
1202  void *cci_value = NULL;
1203  int cci_rc = 0;
1204  T_CCI_ERROR cci_err_buf;
1205  short i;
1206  unsigned long j;
1207  unsigned long h;
1208  DescInfo desc_info;
1209  unsigned short *ParamOperationArrayPtr, *ParamStatusArrayPtr;
1210  unsigned long ProcessedParamNum;
1211  unsigned long *ProcessedParamNumPtr = NULL;
1212  int RevisedParamPos;
1213  char flag_cci_exec = 0;
1214  char flag_stmt_need_data = 0;
1215  char flag_error = 0;
1216 
1217  char *pt_pos, *pt_val;
1218  char pos_buf[128], val_buf[128];
1219  ParamArray *array_of_param_array = NULL;
1220  ParamArray *array_of_oid_param_array = NULL;
1221  T_CCI_QUERY_RESULT *qr;
1222  int res;
1223  int update_count;
1224  const char *err_msg;
1225 
1226  void *value_ptr;
1227  long *ind_ptr;
1228  long *octet_len_ptr;
1229 
1230 
1231 
1232  // Init
1233  reset_result_set (stmt);
1234 
1235  stmt->result_type = QUERY;
1236 
1237 
1238  odbc_get_desc_field (stmt->apd, 0, SQL_DESC_COUNT, &count, 0, NULL);
1239  valid_param_count = MIN (stmt->param_number, count);
1240 
1241  if (stmt->apd->array_size == 1)
1242  {
1243  /* cursor가 sensitive할 경우 SQL_ATTR_ROW_ARRAY_SIZE와 fetch_size를 일치시킨다. connection handle(or DSN)의
1244  * fetch_size는 의미를 상실한다. */
1245  if (stmt->attr_cursor_sensitivity == SQL_SENSITIVE)
1246  {
1247  cci_fetch_size (stmt->stmthd, stmt->ard->array_size);
1248  }
1249 
1250  for (i = 1; i <= valid_param_count; ++i)
1251  {
1252  RevisedParamPos = revised_param_pos (stmt->revised_sql.org_param_pos, i);
1253 
1254  /* APD record */
1255  get_appl_desc_info (stmt->apd, i, &desc_info);
1256 
1257  /* IPD Record */
1258  odbc_get_desc_field (stmt->ipd, i, SQL_DESC_CONCISE_TYPE, &sql_type, 0, NULL);
1259 
1260  a_type = odbc_type_to_cci_a_type (desc_info.type);
1261  u_type = odbc_type_to_cci_u_type (sql_type);
1262 
1263  recalculate_bind_pointer (&desc_info, 1, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr,
1264  (UINT_PTR *) & octet_len_ptr);
1265 
1266  if (octet_len_ptr)
1267  {
1268  desc_info.length = *octet_len_ptr;
1269  }
1270  else
1271  odbc_get_desc_field (stmt->ipd, i, SQL_DESC_LENGTH, &(desc_info.length), 0, NULL);
1272 
1273  if (ind_ptr != NULL && *ind_ptr == SQL_NULL_DATA)
1274  {
1275  cci_rc = cci_bind_param (stmt->stmthd, RevisedParamPos, a_type, NULL, u_type, 0);
1276  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
1277  }
1278  else if (ind_ptr != NULL && IND_IS_DATA_AT_EXEC (*ind_ptr))
1279  {
1280  stmt->data_at_exec_state = STMT_NEED_DATA;
1281  }
1282  else
1283  {
1284  /*--
1285  * cci_bind_param()을 사용할 때 SQLBindParam()에 의한 value pointer
1286  * 를 바로 사용할 수 없다. 왜냐면 SQLBindParam()에 의한 value pointer
1287  * 와 cci_bind_param()에서 사용하는 value pointer사이에는 type conversion
1288  * 등이 발생하기 때문이다.
1289  *--*/
1290  cci_value =
1291  odbc_value_to_cci (value_ptr, desc_info.type, desc_info.length, desc_info.precision, desc_info.scale);
1292  if (cci_value == NULL)
1293  {
1294  odbc_set_diag (stmt->diag, "HY000", 0, "Fail to convert odbc value to cci value");
1295  goto error;
1296  }
1297 
1298 
1299  // oid string checking
1300  if (a_type == CCI_A_TYPE_STR && (u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_CHAR || u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_VARNCHAR))
1301  {
1302  if (is_oidstr (cci_value) == _TRUE_)
1303  {
1304  u_type = CCI_U_TYPE_OBJECT;
1305  }
1306  }
1307 
1308  cci_rc = cci_bind_param (stmt->stmthd, RevisedParamPos, a_type, cci_value, u_type, 0);
1309  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
1310 
1311  NA_FREE (cci_value);
1312  }
1313  }
1314 
1315  // oid param bind
1316  if (stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_num > 0)
1317  {
1318  pt_pos = stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_pos;
1319  pt_val = stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_val;
1320  while (element_from_setstring (&pt_pos, pos_buf) > 0)
1321  {
1322  RevisedParamPos = atoi (pos_buf);
1323  element_from_setstring (&pt_val, val_buf);
1324  cci_rc = cci_bind_param (stmt->stmthd, RevisedParamPos, CCI_A_TYPE_STR, val_buf, CCI_U_TYPE_OBJECT, 0);
1325  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
1326  }
1327  }
1328 
1329  if (stmt->data_at_exec_state == STMT_NEED_DATA)
1330  {
1331  flag_stmt_need_data = 1;
1332  }
1333  else
1334  {
1335  flag_cci_exec = get_flag_of_cci_execute (stmt);
1336  cci_rc = cci_execute (stmt->stmthd, flag_cci_exec, 0, &cci_err_buf);
1337  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
1338 
1339  stmt->tpl_number = cci_rc;
1340  }
1341 
1342  // resource release
1343  NA_FREE (cci_value);
1344 
1345  }
1346  else
1347  { /* ARRAY binding & query for update */
1348  odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_PARAM_STATUS_PTR, &ParamStatusArrayPtr, 0, NULL);
1349  odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_PARAM_OPERATION_PTR, &ParamOperationArrayPtr, 0, NULL);
1350 
1351  if (RESULTSET_STMT_TYPE (stmt->stmt_type))
1352  {
1353  // multi result set
1354  odbc_set_diag (stmt->diag, "HY000", 0, "The driver " "does not support multi result set.");
1355  goto error;
1356  }
1357 
1358  for (h = 1, ProcessedParamNum = 0; h <= stmt->apd->array_size; ++h)
1359  {
1360  if (ParamOperationArrayPtr != NULL && ParamOperationArrayPtr[h - 1] == SQL_PARAM_IGNORE)
1361  {
1362  if (ParamStatusArrayPtr != NULL)
1363  ParamStatusArrayPtr[h - 1] = SQL_PARAM_UNUSED;
1364  continue;
1365  }
1366  else
1367  {
1368  if (ParamStatusArrayPtr != NULL)
1369  ParamStatusArrayPtr[h - 1] = SQL_PARAM_SUCCESS;
1370  }
1371  ++ProcessedParamNum;
1372  }
1373 
1374  if (valid_param_count > 0)
1375  {
1376  array_of_param_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (ParamArray) * valid_param_count);
1377  memset (array_of_param_array, 0, sizeof (ParamArray) * valid_param_count);
1378  }
1379 
1380  cci_bind_param_array_size (stmt->stmthd, ProcessedParamNum);
1381 
1382 
1383  for (i = 1; i <= valid_param_count; ++i)
1384  {
1385  RevisedParamPos = revised_param_pos (stmt->revised_sql.org_param_pos, i);
1386 
1387  /* APD record */
1388  get_appl_desc_info (stmt->apd, i, &desc_info);
1389 
1390  /* IPD Record */
1391  odbc_get_desc_field (stmt->ipd, i, SQL_DESC_CONCISE_TYPE, &sql_type, 0, NULL);
1392 
1393  a_type = odbc_type_to_cci_a_type (desc_info.type);
1394  u_type = odbc_type_to_cci_u_type (sql_type);
1395 
1396 
1397  array_of_param_array[i - 1].value_type = a_type;
1398 
1399  make_param_array (stmt, i, &desc_info, &array_of_param_array[i - 1], ProcessedParamNum);
1400 
1401 
1402  // oid string checking
1403  if (a_type == CCI_A_TYPE_STR && (u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_CHAR || u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_VARNCHAR))
1404  {
1405  if (is_oidstr_array (array_of_param_array[i - 1].value_array, ProcessedParamNum) == _TRUE_)
1406  {
1407  u_type = CCI_U_TYPE_OBJECT;
1408  }
1409  }
1410 
1411  cci_rc =
1412  cci_bind_param_array (stmt->stmthd, RevisedParamPos, a_type, array_of_param_array[i - 1].value_array,
1413  array_of_param_array[i - 1].ind_array, u_type);
1414  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
1415  }
1416 
1417 
1418  // oid param bind
1419  if (stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_num > 0)
1420  {
1421  array_of_oid_param_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (ParamArray) * stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_num);
1422  memset (array_of_oid_param_array, 0, sizeof (ParamArray) * stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_num);
1423 
1424 
1425  pt_pos = stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_pos;
1426  pt_val = stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_val;
1427 
1428  for (i = 0; element_from_setstring (&pt_pos, pos_buf) > 0; ++i)
1429  {
1430  array_of_oid_param_array[i].value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (void *) * ProcessedParamNum);
1431  array_of_oid_param_array[i].ind_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (int) * ProcessedParamNum);
1432  memset (array_of_oid_param_array[i].ind_array, 0, sizeof (int) * ProcessedParamNum);
1433 
1434  RevisedParamPos = atoi (pos_buf);
1435  element_from_setstring (&pt_val, val_buf);
1436 
1437  for (j = 0; j < ProcessedParamNum; ++j)
1438  {
1439  ((char **) array_of_oid_param_array[i].value_array)[j] = UT_MAKE_STRING (val_buf, -1);
1440  }
1441 
1442  cci_rc =
1443  cci_bind_param_array (stmt->stmthd, RevisedParamPos, CCI_A_TYPE_STR,
1444  array_of_oid_param_array[i].value_array, array_of_oid_param_array[i].ind_array,
1445  CCI_U_TYPE_OBJECT);
1446 
1447  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
1448  }
1449  }
1450 
1451 
1452  cci_rc = cci_execute_array (stmt->stmthd, &qr, &cci_err_buf);
1453  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
1454 
1455  res = cci_rc;
1456 
1457  stmt->tpl_number = 0;
1458 
1459  for (i = 1, j = 0, ProcessedParamNum = 0; i <= res; ++i, ++j)
1460  {
1461  if (ParamStatusArrayPtr[j] == SQL_PARAM_UNUSED)
1462  {
1463  ++j;
1464  }
1465  update_count = CCI_QUERY_RESULT_RESULT (qr, i);
1466  if (update_count < 0)
1467  {
1468  err_msg = CCI_QUERY_RESULT_ERR_MSG (qr, i);
1469  ParamStatusArrayPtr[j] = SQL_PARAM_ERROR;
1470  }
1471  else
1472  {
1473  stmt->tpl_number += update_count;
1474  ParamStatusArrayPtr[j] = SQL_PARAM_SUCCESS;
1475  ++ProcessedParamNum;
1476  }
1477  }
1478  cci_query_result_free (qr, res);
1479  free_param_array (array_of_param_array, valid_param_count, ProcessedParamNum);
1480  free_param_array (array_of_oid_param_array, stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_num, ProcessedParamNum);
1481 
1482  // set processed parameters number
1483  odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_PARAMS_PROCESSED_PTR, &ProcessedParamNumPtr, 0, NULL);
1484  if (ProcessedParamNumPtr != NULL)
1485  *ProcessedParamNumPtr = ProcessedParamNum;
1486 
1487  if (stmt->tpl_number == 0 && (stmt->stmt_type == CUBRID_STMT_UPDATE || stmt->stmt_type == CUBRID_STMT_DELETE))
1488  {
1489  if (stmt->conn->env->attr_odbc_version == SQL_OV_ODBC2)
1490  {
1491  return ODBC_SUCCESS; // for 2.x backward compatibility
1492  }
1493  else
1494  {
1495  return ODBC_NO_DATA;
1496  }
1497  }
1498 
1499 
1500  }
1501 
1502  if (flag_stmt_need_data != 0)
1503  return ODBC_NEED_DATA;
1504 
1505  if (!RESULTSET_STMT_TYPE (stmt->stmt_type))
1506  {
1507  odbc_auto_commit (stmt->conn);
1508  }
1509 
1510  return ODBC_SUCCESS;
1511 
1512 cci_error:
1513  if (cci_rc < 0)
1514  odbc_set_diag_by_cci (stmt->diag, cci_rc, &cci_err_buf);
1515 error:
1516  NA_FREE (cci_value);
1517  return ODBC_ERROR;
1518 }
1519 
1520 
1521 /************************************************************************
1522 * name: odbc_param_data
1523 * arguments:
1524 * returns/side-effects:
1525 * description:
1526 * NOTE:
1527 ************************************************************************/
1528 
1529 PUBLIC RETCODE
1530 odbc_param_data (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, void **valueptr_ptr)
1531 {
1532  short param;
1533  short sql_type;
1534  T_CCI_A_TYPE a_type;
1535  T_CCI_U_TYPE u_type;
1536  void *c_value = NULL, *sql_value = NULL;
1537  // long *ind_value_ptr;
1538  void *cci_value = NULL;
1539  int cci_rc;
1540  T_CCI_ERROR cci_err_buf;
1541  short i;
1542  char flag_cci_exec = 0;
1543  DescInfo desc_info;
1544  int RevisedParamPos;
1545 
1546  if (valueptr_ptr == NULL)
1547  {
1548  odbc_set_diag (stmt->diag, "HY009", 0, NULL);
1549  goto error;
1550  }
1551 
1552  // odbc_execute의 putting param data 과정과 같다.
1553  if (stmt->param_data.index != 0)
1554  {
1555  i = stmt->param_data.index;
1556 
1557  /* APD record */
1558  get_appl_desc_info (stmt->apd, i, &desc_info);
1559 
1560  /* IPD Record */
1561  odbc_get_desc_field (stmt->ipd, i, SQL_DESC_CONCISE_TYPE, &sql_type, 0, NULL);
1562 
1563  a_type = odbc_type_to_cci_a_type (desc_info.type);
1564  u_type = odbc_type_to_cci_u_type (sql_type);
1565 
1566 
1567  cci_value =
1568  odbc_value_to_cci (stmt->param_data.val.value, desc_info.type, stmt->param_data.val.usedSize,
1569  desc_info.precision, desc_info.scale);
1570 
1571  if (cci_value == NULL)
1572  {
1573  odbc_set_diag (stmt->diag, "HY000", 0, "Fail to convert odbc value to cci value");
1574  goto error;
1575  }
1576 
1577  /*--
1578  * cci_bind_param()을 사용할 때 SQLBindParam()에 의한 value pointer
1579  * 를 바로 사용할 수 없다. 왜냐면 SQLBindParam()에 의한 value pointer
1580  * 와 cci_bind_param()에서 사용하는 value pointer사이에는 type conversion
1581  * 등이 발생하기 때문이다.
1582  *--*/
1583  RevisedParamPos = revised_param_pos (stmt->revised_sql.org_param_pos, i);
1584  cci_rc = cci_bind_param (stmt->stmthd, RevisedParamPos, a_type, cci_value, u_type, 0);
1585  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
1586 
1587  NA_FREE (cci_value);
1588 
1589  // reset column data
1590  FreeStr (&stmt->param_data.val);
1591  stmt->param_data.index = 0;
1592  }
1593 
1594  if (stmt->data_at_exec_state == STMT_NEED_NO_MORE_DATA)
1595  {
1596  return ODBC_SUCCESS;
1597  }
1598  else if (stmt->data_at_exec_state == STMT_NEED_DATA)
1599  {
1600  /* Start of Data at exec */
1601  param = next_param_data_at_exec (stmt, 0);
1602  }
1603  else
1604  {
1605  param = next_param_data_at_exec (stmt, stmt->data_at_exec_state);
1606  }
1607 
1608  if (param >= 0)
1609  {
1610  /* data_at_exec 상태에 있는 parameter가 존재 */
1611  stmt->data_at_exec_state = param;
1612  stmt->param_data.index = param;
1613 
1614  // spec에서는 SQLBindCol에 의한 data ptr도 얻어올 수 있다고 언급하는데,
1615  // 이해하기 힘들다. SQLBindParam에 대해서만 얻어온다.
1616  odbc_get_desc_field (stmt->apd, param, SQL_DESC_DATA_PTR, valueptr_ptr, 0, NULL);
1617 
1618  return ODBC_NEED_DATA;
1619  }
1620 
1621  // indicator가 data_at_exec인 모든 param에 대해서 SQLPutData가 끝난 상태 // execute를 실행한다. stmt->data_at_exec_state = STMT_NEED_NO_MORE_DATA; flag_cci_exec = get_flag_of_cci_execute (stmt); cci_rc = cci_execute (stmt->stmthd, flag_cci_exec, 0, &cci_err_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error); stmt->tpl_number = cci_rc; if (stmt->tpl_number == 0 && (stmt->stmt_type == CUBRID_STMT_UPDATE || stmt->stmt_type == CUBRID_STMT_DELETE)) { if (stmt->conn->env->attr_odbc_version == SQL_OV_ODBC2) { return ODBC_SUCCESS; // for 2.x backward compatibility } else { return ODBC_NO_DATA; } } return ODBC_SUCCESS; cci_error: if (cci_rc < 0) odbc_set_diag_by_cci (stmt->diag, cci_rc, &cci_err_buf); error: FreeStr (&stmt->param_data.val); stmt->param_data.index = 0; NA_FREE (cci_value); return ODBC_ERROR; } /************************************************************************ * name: odbc_put_data * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * data_at_exec parameter를 위해서 stmt->param_data에 data를 적재한다. * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PUBLIC RETCODE odbc_put_data (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, void *data_ptr, SQLLEN strlen_or_ind) { MemcatImproved (&stmt->param_data.val, data_ptr, (int) strlen_or_ind); return ODBC_SUCCESS; } /************************************************************************ * name: odbc_close_cursor * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PUBLIC RETCODE odbc_close_cursor (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt) { if (stmt->stmthd > 0) { cci_close_req_handle (stmt->stmthd); stmt->stmthd = -1; if (stmt->result_type != TYPE_INFO) { odbc_auto_commit (stmt->conn); } } // reset result set reset_result_set (stmt); // reset_cursor_state(stmt); return ODBC_SUCCESS; } /************************************************************************ * name: odbc_cancel * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * 1. Canceling Functions that Need Data * More functions * Canceling Asynchronous Processing * Canceling Functions in Multithread Applications * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PUBLIC RETCODE odbc_cancel (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt) { if (stmt->data_at_exec_state != STMT_NEED_NO_MORE_DATA) { // reset column data FreeStr (&stmt->param_data.val); stmt->param_data.index = 0; stmt->data_at_exec_state = STMT_NEED_DATA; } else if (stmt->attr_async_enable == SQL_ASYNC_ENABLE_ON) { /* CHECK : 이로 인해서 발생하는 현상은? */ if (stmt->stmthd > 0) { cci_close_req_handle (stmt->stmthd); stmt->stmthd = -1; } } return ODBC_SUCCESS; } /************************************************************************ * name: odbc_bulk_operations * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PUBLIC RETCODE odbc_bulk_operations (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, short operation) { RETCODE rc; unsigned long row_array_size; SQLSETPOSIROW i; unsigned long update_count = 0; unsigned long *RowFetchedPtr; short j; DescInfo *desc_info_ptr = NULL, bookmark_desc_info; void *value_ptr; long *ind_ptr; long bookmark; T_CCI_A_TYPE a_type; int cci_rc = 0; T_CCI_ERROR cci_err_buf; void *cci_value = NULL; char err_flag = 0; char init_flag = 0; /* if flag = 1, that is not first condition */ unsigned short *RowStatusPtr; char query_buf[BUF_SIZE]; char buf[BUF_SIZE]; char param_buf[BUF_SIZE]; char attr_name[NAMEBUFLEN]; row_array_size = stmt->ard->array_size; odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_ROW_STATUS_PTR, &RowStatusPtr, 0, NULL); odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_ROWS_FETCHED_PTR, &RowFetchedPtr, 0, NULL); get_appl_desc_info (stmt->ard, 0, &bookmark_desc_info); desc_info_ptr = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (DescInfo) * stmt->ard->max_count); for (j = 1; j <= stmt->ard->max_count; ++j) { get_appl_desc_info (stmt->ard, j, &desc_info_ptr[j - 1]); } switch (operation) { case SQL_UPDATE_BY_BOOKMARK: for (i = 1; i <= row_array_size; ++i) { recalculate_bind_pointer (&bookmark_desc_info, i, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); bookmark = *((long *) value_ptr); for (j = 1; j <= stmt->ard->max_count; ++j) { recalculate_bind_pointer (&desc_info_ptr[j - 1], i, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); a_type = odbc_type_to_cci_a_type (desc_info_ptr[j - 1].type); if (*ind_ptr == SQL_COLUMN_IGNORE) { continue; } else if (*ind_ptr == SQL_NULL_DATA) { cci_rc = cci_cursor_update (stmt->stmthd, bookmark, j, a_type, (void *) NULL, &cci_err_buf); if (cci_rc < 0) { odbc_set_diag_by_cci (stmt->diag, cci_rc, &cci_err_buf); err_flag = 1; } } else { cci_value = odbc_value_to_cci (value_ptr, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].type, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].length, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].precision, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].scale); cci_rc = cci_cursor_update (stmt->stmthd, bookmark, j, a_type, value_ptr, &cci_err_buf); if (cci_rc < 0) { odbc_set_diag_by_cci (stmt->diag, cci_rc, &cci_err_buf); err_flag = 1; } NA_FREE (cci_value); } } ++update_count; RowStatusPtr[i - 1] = SQL_ROW_UPDATED; } break; case SQL_DELETE_BY_BOOKMARK: for (i = 1; i <= row_array_size; ++i) { recalculate_bind_pointer (&bookmark_desc_info, i, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); bookmark = *((long *) value_ptr); rc = delete_row_by_cursor_pos (stmt, bookmark); ERROR_GOTO (rc, delete_error); ++update_count; RowStatusPtr[i - 1] = SQL_ROW_DELETED; continue; delete_error: RowStatusPtr[i - 1] = SQL_ROW_ERROR; err_flag = 1; } break; case SQL_ADD: /* 주의1 :select의 결과가 하나의 table에서 기인할 때만 유효하다. 그렇지 않은 경우 오작동 주의2 : * base_column_name이 지원되지 않으므로 select attribute 에 alias걸면 안된다. */ { int addhd = -1; int attr_num; int cci_rc; T_CCI_ERROR cci_err_buf; short sql_type; T_CCI_A_TYPE a_type; T_CCI_U_TYPE u_type; void *cci_value = NULL; RETCODE rc; for (i = 1; i <= row_array_size; ++i) { recalculate_bind_pointer (&bookmark_desc_info, i, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); bookmark = *((long *) value_ptr); init_flag = 0; sprintf (query_buf, "insert into %s(", stmt->ird->records->table_name); sprintf (param_buf, " values("); for (j = 1, attr_num = 0; j <= stmt->ard->max_count; ++j) { recalculate_bind_pointer (&desc_info_ptr[j - 1], i, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); if (*ind_ptr == SQL_COLUMN_IGNORE) { continue; } else { rc = odbc_get_desc_field (stmt->ird, j, SQL_DESC_BASE_COLUMN_NAME, attr_name, sizeof (attr_name), NULL); if (init_flag == 1) { sprintf (buf, ", %s", attr_name); strcat (param_buf, ", ?"); } else { sprintf (buf, "%s", attr_name); strcat (param_buf, "?"); init_flag = 1; } strcat (query_buf, buf); ++attr_num; } } strcat (query_buf, ") "); strcat (param_buf, ");"); strcat (query_buf, param_buf); cci_rc = cci_prepare (stmt->conn->connhd, query_buf, 0, &cci_err_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, add_error); addhd = cci_rc; for (j = 1, attr_num = 0; j <= stmt->ard->max_count; ++j) { recalculate_bind_pointer (&desc_info_ptr[j - 1], i, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); odbc_get_desc_field (stmt->ird, j, SQL_DESC_CONCISE_TYPE, &sql_type, 0, NULL); a_type = odbc_type_to_cci_a_type (desc_info_ptr[j - 1].type); u_type = odbc_type_to_cci_u_type (sql_type); if (*ind_ptr == SQL_COLUMN_IGNORE) { continue; } else if (*ind_ptr == SQL_NULL_DATA) { cci_rc = cci_bind_param (addhd, j, a_type, NULL, u_type, 0); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, add_error); } else { cci_value = odbc_value_to_cci (value_ptr, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].type, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].length, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].precision, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].scale); if (cci_value == NULL) { goto add_error; } // oid string checking if (a_type == CCI_A_TYPE_STR && (u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_CHAR || u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_VARNCHAR)) { if (is_oidstr (cci_value) == _TRUE_) { u_type = CCI_U_TYPE_OBJECT; } } cci_rc = cci_bind_param (addhd, j, a_type, cci_value, u_type, 0); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, add_error); NA_FREE (cci_value); } } cci_rc = cci_execute (addhd, 0, 0, &cci_err_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, add_error); if (addhd > 0) { cci_close_req_handle (addhd); addhd = -1; } ++update_count; RowStatusPtr[i - 1] = SQL_ROW_ADDED; continue; add_error: NA_FREE (cci_value); if (addhd > 0) { cci_close_req_handle (addhd); addhd = -1; } RowStatusPtr[i - 1] = SQL_ROW_ERROR; err_flag = 1; } } break; case SQL_FETCH_BY_BOOKMARK: /* array size와 무관하게 설정된 bookmark에 의해서 한 row씩 fetch 해 와야 함. */ odbc_set_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_ROW_ARRAY_SIZE, (void *) 1, 0, 1); for (i = 1; i <= row_array_size; ++i) { recalculate_bind_pointer (&bookmark_desc_info, i, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); bookmark = *((long *) value_ptr); // cursor의 위치는 그대로. rc = odbc_fetch (stmt, SQL_FETCH_ABSOLUTE, bookmark, (long) i - 1, 1); if (rc < 0) { err_flag = 1; } else { ++update_count; } } odbc_set_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_ROW_ARRAY_SIZE, (void *) row_array_size, 0, 1); break; default: break; } NC_FREE (desc_info_ptr); *RowFetchedPtr = update_count; if (err_flag == 1) return ODBC_ERROR; return ODBC_SUCCESS; } /************************************************************************ * name: odbc_set_pos * arguments: * lock_type - ignored... * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: * - refresh일 때는 operation이 반영이 안된다. * - 누군가 bookmark를 조정하면 오작동한다. 절대로 bookmark를 조절해서는 * 안된다. ************************************************************************/ PUBLIC RETCODE odbc_set_pos (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, SQLSETPOSIROW row_number, SQLUSMALLINT operation, SQLUSMALLINT lock_type) { RETCODE rc; DescInfo *desc_info_ptr = NULL, bookmark_desc_info; unsigned short *RowOperationPtr; unsigned short *RowStatusPtr; unsigned long row_array_size; SQLSETPOSIROW i; short max_col_num, j; char error_flag; row_array_size = stmt->ard->array_size; max_col_num = stmt->ard->max_count; odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_ROW_STATUS_PTR, &RowStatusPtr, 0, NULL); odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_ROW_OPERATION_PTR, &RowOperationPtr, 0, NULL); get_appl_desc_info (stmt->ard, 0, &bookmark_desc_info); switch (operation) { case SQL_POSITION: /* There is no operation. Just emulation. */ break; case SQL_REFRESH: // cursor의 위치는 그대로. odbc_fetch (stmt, SQL_FETCH_RELATIVE, 0, 0, 1); break; case SQL_UPDATE: desc_info_ptr = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (DescInfo) * max_col_num); for (j = 1; j <= max_col_num; ++j) { get_appl_desc_info (stmt->ard, j, &desc_info_ptr[j - 1]); } if (row_number == 0) { for (i = 0; i < row_array_size; ++i) { if (RowOperationPtr[i] == SQL_ROW_IGNORE) { continue; } rc = odbc_set_pos_update (stmt, &bookmark_desc_info, desc_info_ptr, i + 1); if (rc < 0) { error_flag = 1; RowStatusPtr[i] = SQL_ROW_ERROR; } else { RowStatusPtr[i] = SQL_ROW_UPDATED; } } } else { rc = odbc_set_pos_update (stmt, &bookmark_desc_info, desc_info_ptr, row_number); if (rc < 0) { error_flag = 1; RowStatusPtr[row_number - 1] = SQL_ROW_ERROR; } else { RowStatusPtr[row_number - 1] = SQL_ROW_UPDATED; } } NC_FREE (desc_info_ptr); break; case SQL_DELETE: if (row_number == 0) { for (i = 0; i < row_array_size; ++i) { if (RowOperationPtr[i] == SQL_ROW_IGNORE) { continue; } rc = odbc_set_pos_delete (stmt, &bookmark_desc_info, i + 1); if (rc < 0) { error_flag = 1; RowStatusPtr[i] = SQL_ROW_ERROR; } else { RowStatusPtr[i] = SQL_ROW_DELETED; } } } else { rc = odbc_set_pos_delete (stmt, &bookmark_desc_info, row_number); if (rc < 0) { error_flag = 1; RowStatusPtr[row_number - 1] = SQL_ROW_ERROR; } else { RowStatusPtr[row_number - 1] = SQL_ROW_DELETED; } } break; } if (error_flag == 1) return ODBC_ERROR; return ODBC_SUCCESS; } /************************************************************************ * name: reset_result_set * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: * IRD는 SQLPrepare 시점에서 이루어지므로, 여기서 IRD를 delete해서는 * 안된다. 왜냐면 SQLExecute도 reset_result_set을 사용하고, * SQLCloseCursor시 IRD가 delete되지 않기 때문이다. ************************************************************************/ PUBLIC void reset_result_set (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt) { if (stmt->result_type == NULL_RESULT) return; // delete catalog result set if (stmt->catalog_result.value != NULL) { free_catalog_result (stmt->catalog_result.value, stmt->result_type); stmt->catalog_result.value = NULL; stmt->catalog_result.current = NULL; } // reset result set state stmt->result_type = NULL_RESULT; stmt->data_at_exec_state = STMT_NEED_NO_MORE_DATA; stmt->tpl_number = 0; stmt->current_tpl_pos = 0; NA_FREE (stmt->cursor); // reset column data free_column_data (&stmt->column_data, RESET); } /************************************************************************ * name: create_ird * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PUBLIC void create_ird (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, T_CCI_COL_INFO * cci_col_info, int column_number) { T_CCI_U_TYPE cci_u_type; short col_type; int col_scale; int col_precision; short col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE_UNKNOWN; short col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_READONLY; char *table_name; char *col_name; short i; if (stmt == NULL || cci_col_info == NULL) return; if (cci_col_info != NULL) { if (GET_STAT_STMT_TYPE (stmt->stmt_type)) { col_type = SQL_VARCHAR; col_precision = MAX_CUBRID_CHAR_LEN; col_scale = 0; col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE_UNKNOWN; col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_READONLY; col_name = "GET_STAT"; odbc_set_ird (stmt, 1, col_type, "", col_name, col_precision, (short) col_scale, col_nullable, col_updatable); } else if (METHOD_STMT_TYPE (stmt->stmt_type)) { col_type = SQL_VARCHAR; col_precision = MAX_CUBRID_CHAR_LEN; col_scale = 0; col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE_UNKNOWN; col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_READONLY; col_name = "METHOD_RESULT"; odbc_set_ird (stmt, 1, col_type, "", col_name, col_precision, (short) col_scale, col_nullable, col_updatable); } else { // CUBRID_STMT_SELECT if (stmt->attr_use_bookmark == SQL_UB_VARIABLE) { create_bookmark_ird (stmt); } if (IS_UPDATABLE (stmt->attr_cursor_type)) { if (cci_is_updatable (stmt->stmthd)) { col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_WRITE; } else { col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_READONLY; stmt->attr_concurrency = SQL_CONCUR_READ_ONLY; stmt->attr_cursor_sensitivity = SQL_INSENSITIVE; stmt->attr_cursor_type = SQL_CURSOR_STATIC; } } for (i = 1; i <= (signed) column_number; ++i) { cci_u_type = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_TYPE (cci_col_info, i); // OBJECT는 string으로 bind되기 때문에 display를 위해서 precision을 // 32로 설정하였다. if (cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_OBJECT) { cci_u_type = CCI_U_TYPE_CHAR; col_precision = 32; col_scale = 0; } else if (CCI_IS_COLLECTION_TYPE (cci_u_type)) { /* XXX : deprecated cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_SET || cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_MULTISET || cci_u_type * == CCI_U_TYPE_SEQUENCE ) { */ cci_u_type = CCI_U_TYPE_STRING; col_precision = MAX_CUBRID_CHAR_LEN; col_scale = 0; } else { col_precision = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_PRECISION (cci_col_info, i); // revise col_precision col_precision = (col_precision < 0) ? DEFAULT_COL_PRECISION : col_precision; #ifdef DELPHI col_type = odbc_type_by_cci (cci_u_type, col_precision); #endif if (cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_STRING || cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_CHAR) { if (col_precision >= stmt->conn->max_string_length) col_precision = stmt->conn->max_string_length; } col_scale = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_SCALE (cci_col_info, i); } col_name = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_NAME (cci_col_info, i); table_name = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_CLASS_NAME (cci_col_info, i); if (CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_IS_NON_NULL (cci_col_info, i) == 0) { // nullable col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE; } else if (CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_IS_NON_NULL (cci_col_info, i) == 1) { col_nullable = SQL_NO_NULLS; } else { col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE_UNKNOWN; } #ifndef DELPHI col_type = odbc_type_by_cci (cci_u_type, col_precision); #endif odbc_set_ird (stmt, i, col_type, table_name, col_name, col_precision, (short) col_scale, col_nullable, col_updatable); } } } } /************************************************************************ * name: next_param_data_at_exec * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * * description: * APD에서 param_pos이후의 record에 대해서 indicator가 DATA_AT_EXEC 인 것을 * 찾는다. 찾으면 record number, else -1 * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE short next_param_data_at_exec (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, short param_pos) { ODBC_RECORD *record = NULL; int i; if (param_pos > stmt->apd->max_count) { return -1; } for (i = param_pos + 1; i <= stmt->apd->max_count; ++i) { record = find_record_from_desc (stmt->apd, i); if (record != NULL) { if (IND_IS_DATA_AT_EXEC (*(record->indicator_ptr))) { return i; } } } return -1; } PUBLIC void free_column_data (COLUMN_DATA * data, int option) { if (data == NULL) return; switch (option) { case INIT: case RESET: case FREE_MEMBER: data->current_pt = NULL; data->column_no = 0; data->remain_length = 0; data->prev_return_status = -1; break; case FREE_ALL: default: data->current_pt = NULL; data->column_no = 0; data->remain_length = 0; data->prev_return_status = -1; UT_FREE (data); break; } } /************************************************************************ * name: get_appl_desc_info * arguments: * col_index - parameter col index, starting from 1 * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void get_appl_desc_info (ODBC_DESC * desc, short col_index, DescInfo * desc_info_ptr) { if (desc == NULL || desc_info_ptr == NULL) return; memset (desc_info_ptr, 0, sizeof (DescInfo)); desc_info_ptr->bind_type = desc->bind_type; /* 0 means single or column wise, >0 means row wise */ if (desc->bind_offset_ptr == NULL) { desc_info_ptr->offset_size = 0; } else { desc_info_ptr->offset_size = *(desc->bind_offset_ptr); } if (desc_info_ptr == NULL) return; odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_CONCISE_TYPE, &(desc_info_ptr->type), 0, NULL); odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_DATA_PTR, &(desc_info_ptr->value_ptr), 0, NULL); odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_INDICATOR_PTR, &(desc_info_ptr->ind_ptr), 0, NULL); odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_OCTET_LENGTH, &(desc_info_ptr->length), 0, NULL); odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_PRECISION, &(desc_info_ptr->precision), 0, NULL); odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_SCALE, &(desc_info_ptr->scale), 0, NULL); odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_OCTET_LENGTH_PTR, &(desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr), 0, NULL); } /************************************************************************ * name: recalculate_bind_pointer * arguments: * row_index - array index, starting from 1 * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void recalculate_bind_pointer (DescInfo * desc_info_ptr, SQLSETPOSIROW row_index, UINT_PTR * value_addr, UINT_PTR * ind_addr, UINT_PTR * octet_len_addr) { long element_size; if (desc_info_ptr->value_ptr == NULL) { (void *) *value_addr = NULL; (long *) *ind_addr = NULL; if (octet_len_addr) { (long *) *octet_len_addr = NULL; } } else { if (desc_info_ptr->bind_type == SQL_PARAM_BIND_BY_COLUMN) { *value_addr = (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->value_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * (desc_info_ptr->length); *ind_addr = (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->ind_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * sizeof (long); if (octet_len_addr) { if (desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr) *octet_len_addr = (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * sizeof (long); else (long *) *octet_len_addr = NULL; } } else { element_size = desc_info_ptr->bind_type; *value_addr = (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->value_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * element_size; *ind_addr = (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->ind_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * element_size; if (octet_len_addr) { if (desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr) *octet_len_addr = (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * element_size; else (long *) *octet_len_addr = NULL; } } } } /************************************************************************ * name: reset_revised_sql * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void reset_revised_sql (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt) { if (stmt == NULL) return; NA_FREE (stmt->revised_sql.sql_text); NA_FREE (stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_pos); NA_FREE (stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_val); NA_FREE (stmt->revised_sql.org_param_pos); stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_num = 0; } /************************************************************************ * name: reset_revised_sql * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE int revised_param_pos (char *param_pos, int index) { int i; short rv; char *pt; char buf[128]; int revised_pos = 0; if (param_pos == NULL) return 0; pt = param_pos; i = 0; while ((rv = element_from_setstring (&pt, buf)) > 0) { ++i; if (i == index) { revised_pos = atoi (buf); break; } } return revised_pos; } /************************************************************************ * name: get_flag_of_cci_prepare * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * flag of cci_execute() * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE char get_flag_of_cci_prepare (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt) { if (stmt == NULL) return 0; if (IS_UPDATABLE (stmt->attr_cursor_type)) { return (CCI_PREPARE_UPDATABLE | CCI_PREPARE_INCLUDE_OID); } return 0; } /************************************************************************ * name: get_flag_of_cci_execute * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * flag of cci_execute() * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE char get_flag_of_cci_execute (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt) { if (stmt == NULL) return 0; return CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL; } /************************************************************************ * name: create_bookmark_ird * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * 0번 ird record는 BOOKMARK를 위한 것이다. * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void create_bookmark_ird (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt) { short verbose_type; long display_size; long octet_length; ODBC_RECORD *record; short type; long precision; short scale; if (stmt == NULL) return; record = find_record_from_desc (stmt->ird, 0); if (record == NULL) { odbc_alloc_record (stmt->ird, &record, 0); } type = SQL_VARBINARY; precision = 4; scale = 0; verbose_type = odbc_concise_to_verbose_type (type); display_size = odbc_display_size (type, precision); octet_length = odbc_octet_length (type, precision); odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_CONCISE_TYPE, (SQLPOINTER) type, 0, 1); odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_TYPE_NAME, (SQLPOINTER) odbc_type_name (type), SQL_NTS, 1); odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_TYPE, (SQLPOINTER) verbose_type, 0, 1); if (IS_STRING_TYPE (type) || IS_BINARY_TYPE (type)) { odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_PRECISION, (SQLPOINTER) 0, 0, 1); // precision에 대해서 정의하고 있지 않다. } else if (odbc_is_valid_sql_date_type (type)) { odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_PRECISION, (SQLPOINTER) 0, 0, 1); // CUBRID은 date type에 대해서 precision(for second)은 0이다. // date type에 대한 length는 char형색의 display size와 같다. } else { odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_PRECISION, (SQLPOINTER) precision, 0, 1); } odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_LENGTH, (SQLPOINTER) display_size, 0, 1); odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_OCTET_LENGTH, (SQLPOINTER) octet_length, 0, 1); odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_SCALE, (SQLPOINTER) scale, 0, 1); odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_DISPLAY_SIZE, (SQLPOINTER) display_size, 0, 1); odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_UNSIGNED, (SQLPOINTER) SQL_TRUE, 0, 1); } /************************************************************************ * name: make_param_array * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: * 이미 param_array에는 memory가 할당된 상태이다. ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void make_param_array (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, short column_index, DescInfo * desc_info, ParamArray * param_array, int array_size) { SQLSETPOSIROW h; unsigned long i; void *value_ptr; long *ind_ptr; void *cci_value = NULL; unsigned short *ParamOperationArrayPtr; odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_PARAM_OPERATION_PTR, &ParamOperationArrayPtr, 0, NULL); memory_alloc_param_array (param_array, array_size); for (h = 1, i = 0; h <= stmt->apd->array_size; ++h) { if (stmt->apd->array_size > 1) { if (ParamOperationArrayPtr != NULL && ParamOperationArrayPtr[h - 1] == SQL_PARAM_IGNORE) { continue; } } recalculate_bind_pointer (desc_info, h, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); if (ind_ptr != NULL && *ind_ptr == SQL_NULL_DATA) { param_array->ind_array[i] = 1; ((char **) param_array->value_array)[i] = NULL; } else { param_array->ind_array[i] = 0; odbc_value_to_cci2 (param_array->value_array, i, value_ptr, desc_info->type, desc_info->length, desc_info->precision, desc_info->scale); } ++i; } } /************************************************************************ * name: * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void memory_alloc_param_array (ParamArray * param_array, int array_size) { param_array->ind_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (int) * array_size); switch (param_array->value_type) { case CCI_A_TYPE_STR: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (char *) * array_size); break; case CCI_A_TYPE_BIGINT: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (__int64) * array_size); break; case CCI_A_TYPE_INT: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (int) * array_size); break; case CCI_A_TYPE_FLOAT: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (float) * array_size); break; case CCI_A_TYPE_DOUBLE: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (double) * array_size); break; case CCI_A_TYPE_BIT: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (T_CCI_BIT) * array_size); break; case CCI_A_TYPE_SET: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (T_CCI_SET) * array_size); break; case CCI_A_TYPE_DATE: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (T_CCI_DATE) * array_size); break; } } /************************************************************************ * name: delete_row_by_cursor_pos * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE RETCODE delete_row_by_cursor_pos (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, unsigned long cursor_pos) { int cci_rc = 0; T_CCI_ERROR cci_err_buf; char oid_buf[32]; cci_rc = cci_cursor (stmt->stmthd, cursor_pos, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &cci_err_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error); cci_rc = cci_fetch (stmt->stmthd, &cci_err_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error); cci_rc = cci_get_cur_oid (stmt->stmthd, oid_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error); cci_rc = cci_oid (stmt->conn->connhd, CCI_OID_DROP, oid_buf, &cci_err_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error); return ODBC_SUCCESS; cci_error: if (cci_rc < 0) odbc_set_diag_by_cci (stmt->diag, cci_rc, &cci_err_buf); return ODBC_ERROR; } /************************************************************************ * name: odbc_set_pos_update * arguments: * row_pos - row position in ard. (starting from 1) * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE RETCODE odbc_set_pos_update (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, DescInfo * bookmark_desc_info_ptr, DescInfo * desc_info_ptr, SQLSETPOSIROW row_pos) { short max_col_num, j; void *value_ptr; long *ind_ptr; long bookmark; T_CCI_A_TYPE a_type; int cci_rc = 0; T_CCI_ERROR cci_err_buf; void *cci_value = NULL; if (stmt == NULL || bookmark_desc_info_ptr == NULL || desc_info_ptr == NULL) return ODBC_ERROR; max_col_num = stmt->ard->max_count; recalculate_bind_pointer (bookmark_desc_info_ptr, row_pos, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); bookmark = *((long *) value_ptr); for (j = 1; j <= stmt->ard->max_count; ++j) { recalculate_bind_pointer (&desc_info_ptr[j - 1], row_pos, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); a_type = odbc_type_to_cci_a_type (desc_info_ptr[j - 1].type); if (*ind_ptr == SQL_COLUMN_IGNORE) { continue; } else if (*ind_ptr == SQL_NULL_DATA) { cci_rc = cci_cursor_update (stmt->stmthd, bookmark, j, a_type, (void *) NULL, &cci_err_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error); } else { cci_value = odbc_value_to_cci (value_ptr, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].type, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].length, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].precision, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].scale); cci_rc = cci_cursor_update (stmt->stmthd, bookmark, j, a_type, value_ptr, &cci_err_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error); NA_FREE (cci_value); } } return ODBC_SUCCESS; cci_error: NA_FREE (cci_value); odbc_set_diag_by_cci (stmt->diag, cci_rc, &cci_err_buf); return ODBC_ERROR; } /************************************************************************ * name: odbc_set_pos_delete * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE RETCODE odbc_set_pos_delete (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, DescInfo * bookmark_desc_info_ptr, SQLSETPOSIROW row_pos) { RETCODE rc; void *value_ptr; long *ind_ptr; long bookmark; if (stmt == NULL) return ODBC_ERROR; recalculate_bind_pointer (bookmark_desc_info_ptr, row_pos, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); bookmark = *((long *) value_ptr); rc = delete_row_by_cursor_pos (stmt, bookmark); if (rc < 0) return ODBC_ERROR; return ODBC_SUCCESS; } /************************************************************************ * name: free_param_array * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void free_param_array (ParamArray * param_ptr, int param_count, int array_count) { int i; int j; char **cpt; T_CCI_BIT *bpt; if (param_ptr == NULL || param_count < 0) return; for (i = 0; i < param_count; ++i) { switch (param_ptr[i].value_type) { case CCI_A_TYPE_STR: cpt = param_ptr[i].value_array; for (j = 0; j < array_count; ++j) { NC_FREE (cpt[j]); } break; case CCI_A_TYPE_BIT: bpt = param_ptr[i].value_array; for (j = 0; j < array_count; ++j) { NC_FREE (bpt[i].buf); } break; } NC_FREE (param_ptr[i].value_array); NC_FREE (param_ptr[i].ind_array); } free (param_ptr); } #ifdef _DEBUG PRIVATE void debug_print_appl_desc (DescInfo * desc_info, void *value_ptr, long *ind_ptr) { switch (desc_info->type) { case SQL_C_SHORT: // for 2.x backward compatibility case SQL_C_SSHORT: case SQL_C_USHORT: printf ("[short] %d ||", *(short *) value_ptr); break; case SQL_C_STINYINT: case SQL_C_UTINYINT: case SQL_C_TINYINT: // for 2.x backward compatibility printf ("[short] %d ||", *(char *) value_ptr); break; case SQL_C_LONG: // for 2.x backward compatibility case SQL_C_SLONG: case SQL_C_ULONG: printf ("[long] %ld || ", *(long *) value_ptr); break; case SQL_C_SBIGINT: case SQL_C_UBIGINT: printf ("[bigint] %lld || ", (long long) (*(__int64 *) value_ptr)); break; /*--------------------------------------------------------------- * floating point type *--------------------------------------------------------------*/ case SQL_C_FLOAT: printf ("[float] %f || ", *(float *) value_ptr); break; case SQL_C_DOUBLE: printf ("[double] %lf || ", *(double *) value_ptr); break; /*--------------------------------------------------------------- * char & binary type *--------------------------------------------------------------*/ case SQL_C_CHAR: printf ("[string] %s || ", (char *) value_ptr); break; } } #endif PRIVATE short default_type_to_c_type (short value_type, short parameter_type) { switch (parameter_type) { case SQL_CHAR: case SQL_VARCHAR: case SQL_LONGVARCHAR: return SQL_C_CHAR; case SQL_WCHAR: case SQL_WVARCHAR: case SQL_WLONGVARCHAR: return SQL_C_WCHAR; case SQL_DECIMAL: case SQL_NUMERIC: return SQL_C_CHAR; case SQL_BIT: return SQL_C_BIT; case SQL_TINYINT: return SQL_C_TINYINT; case SQL_SMALLINT: return SQL_C_SSHORT; case SQL_INTEGER: return SQL_C_SLONG; case SQL_BIGINT: return SQL_C_SBIGINT; case SQL_REAL: return SQL_C_FLOAT; case SQL_FLOAT: case SQL_DOUBLE: return SQL_C_DOUBLE; case SQL_BINARY: case SQL_VARBINARY: case SQL_LONGVARBINARY: return SQL_C_BINARY; case SQL_TYPE_DATE: return SQL_C_TYPE_DATE; case SQL_TYPE_TIME: return SQL_C_TYPE_TIME; case SQL_TYPE_TIMESTAMP: return SQL_C_TYPE_TIMESTAMP; case SQL_GUID: return SQL_C_CHAR; } return value_type; }
1622  // execute를 실행한다.
1623  stmt->data_at_exec_state = STMT_NEED_NO_MORE_DATA;
1624 
1625  flag_cci_exec = get_flag_of_cci_execute (stmt);
1626  cci_rc = cci_execute (stmt->stmthd, flag_cci_exec, 0, &cci_err_buf);
1627  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
1628 
1629  stmt->tpl_number = cci_rc;
1630 
1631  if (stmt->tpl_number == 0 && (stmt->stmt_type == CUBRID_STMT_UPDATE || stmt->stmt_type == CUBRID_STMT_DELETE))
1632  {
1633  if (stmt->conn->env->attr_odbc_version == SQL_OV_ODBC2)
1634  {
1635  return ODBC_SUCCESS; // for 2.x backward compatibility
1636  }
1637  else
1638  {
1639  return ODBC_NO_DATA;
1640  }
1641  }
1642 
1643  return ODBC_SUCCESS;
1644 
1645 cci_error:
1646  if (cci_rc < 0)
1647  odbc_set_diag_by_cci (stmt->diag, cci_rc, &cci_err_buf);
1648 error:
1649  FreeStr (&stmt->param_data.val);
1650  stmt->param_data.index = 0;
1651  NA_FREE (cci_value);
1652  return ODBC_ERROR;
1653 }

1673 /************************************************************************
1674 * name: odbc_close_cursor
1675 * arguments:
1676 * returns/side-effects:
1677 * description:
1678 * NOTE:
1679 ************************************************************************/
1680 PUBLIC RETCODE
1681 odbc_close_cursor (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt)
1682 {
1683  if (stmt->stmthd > 0)
1684  {
1685  cci_close_req_handle (stmt->stmthd);
1686  stmt->stmthd = -1;
1687 
1688  if (stmt->result_type != TYPE_INFO)
1689  {
1690  odbc_auto_commit (stmt->conn);
1691  }
1692  }
1693  // reset result set
1694  reset_result_set (stmt);
1695  // reset_cursor_state(stmt);
1696  return ODBC_SUCCESS;
1697 }

1699 /************************************************************************
1700 * name: odbc_cancel
1701 * arguments:
1702 * returns/side-effects:
1703 * description:
1704 * 1. Canceling Functions that Need Data
1705 * More functions
1706 * Canceling Asynchronous Processing
1707 * Canceling Functions in Multithread Applications
1708 * NOTE:
1709 ************************************************************************/
1710 PUBLIC RETCODE
1711 odbc_cancel (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt)
1712 {
1713 
1714  if (stmt->data_at_exec_state != STMT_NEED_NO_MORE_DATA)
1715  {
1716  // reset column data
1717  FreeStr (&stmt->param_data.val);
1718  stmt->param_data.index = 0;
1719  stmt->data_at_exec_state = STMT_NEED_DATA;
1720  }
1721  else if (stmt->attr_async_enable == SQL_ASYNC_ENABLE_ON)
1722  {
1723  /* CHECK : 이로 인해서 발생하는 현상은? */
1724  if (stmt->stmthd > 0)
1725  {
1726  cci_close_req_handle (stmt->stmthd);
1727  stmt->stmthd = -1;
1728  }
1729  }
1730 
1731  return ODBC_SUCCESS;
1732 }

1734 /************************************************************************
1735 * name: odbc_bulk_operations
1736 * arguments:
1737 * returns/side-effects:
1738 * description:
1739 * NOTE:
1740 ************************************************************************/
1741 PUBLIC RETCODE
1742 odbc_bulk_operations (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, short operation)
1743 {
1744  RETCODE rc;
1745  unsigned long row_array_size;
1746  SQLSETPOSIROW i;
1747  unsigned long update_count = 0;
1748  unsigned long *RowFetchedPtr;
1749  short j;
1750  DescInfo *desc_info_ptr = NULL, bookmark_desc_info;
1751  void *value_ptr;
1752  long *ind_ptr;
1753  long bookmark;
1754  T_CCI_A_TYPE a_type;
1755  int cci_rc = 0;
1756  T_CCI_ERROR cci_err_buf;
1757  void *cci_value = NULL;
1758  char err_flag = 0;
1759  char init_flag = 0; /* if flag = 1, that is not first condition */
1760  unsigned short *RowStatusPtr;
1761  char query_buf[BUF_SIZE];
1762  char buf[BUF_SIZE];
1763  char param_buf[BUF_SIZE];
1764  char attr_name[NAMEBUFLEN];
1765 
1766 
1767  row_array_size = stmt->ard->array_size;
1768 
1769  odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_ROW_STATUS_PTR, &RowStatusPtr, 0, NULL);
1770  odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_ROWS_FETCHED_PTR, &RowFetchedPtr, 0, NULL);
1771 
1772  get_appl_desc_info (stmt->ard, 0, &bookmark_desc_info);
1773 
1774  desc_info_ptr = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (DescInfo) * stmt->ard->max_count);
1775 
1776  for (j = 1; j <= stmt->ard->max_count; ++j)
1777  {
1778  get_appl_desc_info (stmt->ard, j, &desc_info_ptr[j - 1]);
1779  }
1780 
1781 
1782  switch (operation)
1783  {
1784  case SQL_UPDATE_BY_BOOKMARK:
1785  for (i = 1; i <= row_array_size; ++i)
1786  {
1787  recalculate_bind_pointer (&bookmark_desc_info, i, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL);
1788  bookmark = *((long *) value_ptr);
1789 
1790  for (j = 1; j <= stmt->ard->max_count; ++j)
1791  {
1792  recalculate_bind_pointer (&desc_info_ptr[j - 1], i, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr,
1793  NULL);
1794  a_type = odbc_type_to_cci_a_type (desc_info_ptr[j - 1].type);
1795 
1796  if (*ind_ptr == SQL_COLUMN_IGNORE)
1797  {
1798  continue;
1799  }
1800  else if (*ind_ptr == SQL_NULL_DATA)
1801  {
1802  cci_rc = cci_cursor_update (stmt->stmthd, bookmark, j, a_type, (void *) NULL, &cci_err_buf);
1803  if (cci_rc < 0)
1804  {
1805  odbc_set_diag_by_cci (stmt->diag, cci_rc, &cci_err_buf);
1806  err_flag = 1;
1807  }
1808  }
1809  else
1810  {
1811  cci_value =
1812  odbc_value_to_cci (value_ptr, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].type, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].length,
1813  desc_info_ptr[j - 1].precision, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].scale);
1814  cci_rc = cci_cursor_update (stmt->stmthd, bookmark, j, a_type, value_ptr, &cci_err_buf);
1815  if (cci_rc < 0)
1816  {
1817  odbc_set_diag_by_cci (stmt->diag, cci_rc, &cci_err_buf);
1818  err_flag = 1;
1819  }
1820 
1821  NA_FREE (cci_value);
1822  }
1823  }
1824  ++update_count;
1825  RowStatusPtr[i - 1] = SQL_ROW_UPDATED;
1826  }
1827  break;
1828 
1829  case SQL_DELETE_BY_BOOKMARK:
1830  for (i = 1; i <= row_array_size; ++i)
1831  {
1832  recalculate_bind_pointer (&bookmark_desc_info, i, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL);
1833  bookmark = *((long *) value_ptr);
1834 
1835  rc = delete_row_by_cursor_pos (stmt, bookmark);
1836  ERROR_GOTO (rc, delete_error);
1837 
1838  ++update_count;
1839  RowStatusPtr[i - 1] = SQL_ROW_DELETED;
1840  continue;
1841 
1842  delete_error:
1843  RowStatusPtr[i - 1] = SQL_ROW_ERROR;
1844  err_flag = 1;
1845  }
1846  break;
1847 
1848  case SQL_ADD:
1849  /* 주의1 :select의 결과가 하나의 table에서 기인할 때만 유효하다. 그렇지 않은 경우 오작동 주의2 :
1850  * base_column_name이 지원되지 않으므로 select attribute 에 alias걸면 안된다. */
1851  {
1852  int addhd = -1;
1853  int attr_num;
1854  int cci_rc;
1855  T_CCI_ERROR cci_err_buf;
1856  short sql_type;
1857  T_CCI_A_TYPE a_type;
1858  T_CCI_U_TYPE u_type;
1859  void *cci_value = NULL;
1860  RETCODE rc;
1861 
1862 
1863  for (i = 1; i <= row_array_size; ++i)
1864  {
1865  recalculate_bind_pointer (&bookmark_desc_info, i, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL);
1866  bookmark = *((long *) value_ptr);
1867 
1868  init_flag = 0;
1869  sprintf (query_buf, "insert into %s(", stmt->ird->records->table_name);
1870  sprintf (param_buf, " values(");
1871 
1872  for (j = 1, attr_num = 0; j <= stmt->ard->max_count; ++j)
1873  {
1874  recalculate_bind_pointer (&desc_info_ptr[j - 1], i, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr,
1875  NULL);
1876  if (*ind_ptr == SQL_COLUMN_IGNORE)
1877  {
1878  continue;
1879  }
1880  else
1881  {
1882  rc =
1883  odbc_get_desc_field (stmt->ird, j, SQL_DESC_BASE_COLUMN_NAME, attr_name, sizeof (attr_name),
1884  NULL);
1885  if (init_flag == 1)
1886  {
1887  sprintf (buf, ", %s", attr_name);
1888  strcat (param_buf, ", ?");
1889 
1890  }
1891  else
1892  {
1893  sprintf (buf, "%s", attr_name);
1894  strcat (param_buf, "?");
1895  init_flag = 1;
1896  }
1897  strcat (query_buf, buf);
1898  ++attr_num;
1899  }
1900 
1901  }
1902  strcat (query_buf, ") ");
1903  strcat (param_buf, ");");
1904  strcat (query_buf, param_buf);
1905 
1906 
1907  cci_rc = cci_prepare (stmt->conn->connhd, query_buf, 0, &cci_err_buf);
1908  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, add_error);
1909 
1910  addhd = cci_rc;
1911 
1912  for (j = 1, attr_num = 0; j <= stmt->ard->max_count; ++j)
1913  {
1914  recalculate_bind_pointer (&desc_info_ptr[j - 1], i, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr,
1915  NULL);
1916 
1917  odbc_get_desc_field (stmt->ird, j, SQL_DESC_CONCISE_TYPE, &sql_type, 0, NULL);
1918 
1919  a_type = odbc_type_to_cci_a_type (desc_info_ptr[j - 1].type);
1920  u_type = odbc_type_to_cci_u_type (sql_type);
1921 
1922  if (*ind_ptr == SQL_COLUMN_IGNORE)
1923  {
1924  continue;
1925  }
1926  else if (*ind_ptr == SQL_NULL_DATA)
1927  {
1928  cci_rc = cci_bind_param (addhd, j, a_type, NULL, u_type, 0);
1929  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, add_error);
1930  }
1931  else
1932  {
1933  cci_value =
1934  odbc_value_to_cci (value_ptr, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].type, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].length,
1935  desc_info_ptr[j - 1].precision, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].scale);
1936  if (cci_value == NULL)
1937  {
1938  goto add_error;
1939  }
1940  // oid string checking
1941  if (a_type == CCI_A_TYPE_STR && (u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_CHAR || u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_VARNCHAR))
1942  {
1943  if (is_oidstr (cci_value) == _TRUE_)
1944  {
1945  u_type = CCI_U_TYPE_OBJECT;
1946  }
1947  }
1948 
1949  cci_rc = cci_bind_param (addhd, j, a_type, cci_value, u_type, 0);
1950  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, add_error);
1951 
1952  NA_FREE (cci_value);
1953  }
1954 
1955  }
1956 
1957  cci_rc = cci_execute (addhd, 0, 0, &cci_err_buf);
1958  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, add_error);
1959 
1960 
1961  if (addhd > 0)
1962  {
1963  cci_close_req_handle (addhd);
1964  addhd = -1;
1965  }
1966 
1967  ++update_count;
1968  RowStatusPtr[i - 1] = SQL_ROW_ADDED;
1969  continue;
1970 
1971  add_error:
1972  NA_FREE (cci_value);
1973 
1974  if (addhd > 0)
1975  {
1976  cci_close_req_handle (addhd);
1977  addhd = -1;
1978  }
1979  RowStatusPtr[i - 1] = SQL_ROW_ERROR;
1980  err_flag = 1;
1981  }
1982 
1983  }
1984  break;
1985 
1986  case SQL_FETCH_BY_BOOKMARK:
1987  /* array size와 무관하게 설정된 bookmark에 의해서 한 row씩 fetch 해 와야 함. */
1988  odbc_set_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_ROW_ARRAY_SIZE, (void *) 1, 0, 1);
1989 
1990  for (i = 1; i <= row_array_size; ++i)
1991  {
1992  recalculate_bind_pointer (&bookmark_desc_info, i, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL);
1993  bookmark = *((long *) value_ptr);
1994  // cursor의 위치는 그대로.
1995  rc = odbc_fetch (stmt, SQL_FETCH_ABSOLUTE, bookmark, (long) i - 1, 1);
1996  if (rc < 0)
1997  {
1998  err_flag = 1;
1999  }
2000  else
2001  {
2002  ++update_count;
2003  }
2004  }
2005 
2006  odbc_set_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_ROW_ARRAY_SIZE, (void *) row_array_size, 0, 1);
2007  break;
2008 
2009  default:
2010  break;
2011  }
2012 
2013  NC_FREE (desc_info_ptr);
2014 
2015  *RowFetchedPtr = update_count;
2016 
2017  if (err_flag == 1)
2018  return ODBC_ERROR;
2019 
2020  return ODBC_SUCCESS;
2021 }
2022 
2023 /************************************************************************
2024 * name: odbc_set_pos
2025 * arguments:
2026 * lock_type - ignored...
2027 * returns/side-effects:
2028 * description:
2029 * NOTE:
2030 * - refresh일 때는 operation이 반영이 안된다.
2031 * - 누군가 bookmark를 조정하면 오작동한다. 절대로 bookmark를 조절해서는* 안된다. ************************************************************************/ PUBLIC RETCODE odbc_set_pos (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, SQLSETPOSIROW row_number, SQLUSMALLINT operation, SQLUSMALLINT lock_type) { RETCODE rc; DescInfo *desc_info_ptr = NULL, bookmark_desc_info; unsigned short *RowOperationPtr; unsigned short *RowStatusPtr; unsigned long row_array_size; SQLSETPOSIROW i; short max_col_num, j; char error_flag; row_array_size = stmt->ard->array_size; max_col_num = stmt->ard->max_count; odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_ROW_STATUS_PTR, &RowStatusPtr, 0, NULL); odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_ROW_OPERATION_PTR, &RowOperationPtr, 0, NULL); get_appl_desc_info (stmt->ard, 0, &bookmark_desc_info); switch (operation) { case SQL_POSITION: /* There is no operation. Just emulation. */ break; case SQL_REFRESH: // cursor의 위치는 그대로. odbc_fetch (stmt, SQL_FETCH_RELATIVE, 0, 0, 1); break; case SQL_UPDATE: desc_info_ptr = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (DescInfo) * max_col_num); for (j = 1; i < row_array_size; ++i) { if (RowOperationPtr[i] == SQL_ROW_IGNORE) { continue; } rc = odbc_set_pos_delete (stmt, &bookmark_desc_info, i + 1); if (rc < 0) { error_flag = 1; RowStatusPtr[i] = SQL_ROW_ERROR; } } break; } if (error_flag == 1) return ODBC_ERROR; return ODBC_SUCCESS; } /************************************************************************ * name: reset_result_set * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: * IRD는 SQLPrepare 시점에서 이루어지므로, 여기서 IRD를 delete해서는 * 안된다. 왜냐면 SQLExecute도 reset_result_set을 사용하고, * SQLCloseCursor시 IRD가 delete되지 않기 때문이다. ************************************************************************/ PUBLIC void reset_result_set (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt) { if (stmt->result_type == NULL_RESULT) return; } /************************************************************************ * name: create_ird * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PUBLIC void create_ird (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, T_CCI_COL_INFO * cci_col_info, int column_number) { T_CCI_U_TYPE cci_u_type; #endif odbc_set_ird (stmt, i, col_type, table_name, col_name, col_precision, (short) col_scale, col_nullable, col_updatable); } } } } /************************************************************************ * name: next_param_data_at_exec * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * * description: * APD에서 param_pos이후의 record에 대해서 indicator가 DATA_AT_EXEC 인 것을 * 찾는다. 찾으면 record number, else -1 * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE short next_param_data_at_exec (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, short param_pos) { ODBC_RECORD *record = NULL; else (long *) *octet_len_addr = NULL; } } } } /************************************************************************ * name: reset_revised_sql * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void reset_revised_sql (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt) { if (stmt == NULL) return;
