2036 {
2037  RETCODE rc;
2038  DescInfo *desc_info_ptr = NULL, bookmark_desc_info;
2039  unsigned short *RowOperationPtr;
2040  unsigned short *RowStatusPtr;
2041  unsigned long row_array_size;
2042  SQLSETPOSIROW i;
2043  short max_col_num, j;
2044  char error_flag;
2045 
2046  row_array_size = stmt->ard->array_size;
2047  max_col_num = stmt->ard->max_count;
2048 
2049  odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_ROW_STATUS_PTR, &RowStatusPtr, 0, NULL);
2050  odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_ROW_OPERATION_PTR, &RowOperationPtr, 0, NULL);
2051 
2052  get_appl_desc_info (stmt->ard, 0, &bookmark_desc_info);
2053 
2054 
2055 
2056  switch (operation)
2057  {
2058  case SQL_POSITION:
2059  /* There is no operation. Just emulation. */
2060  break;
2061 
2062  case SQL_REFRESH:
2063  // cursor의 위치는 그대로.
2064  odbc_fetch (stmt, SQL_FETCH_RELATIVE, 0, 0, 1);
2065  break;
2066 
2067  case SQL_UPDATE:
2068  desc_info_ptr = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (DescInfo) * max_col_num);
2069 
2070  for (j = 1; j <= max_col_num; ++j)
2071  {
2072  get_appl_desc_info (stmt->ard, j, &desc_info_ptr[j - 1]);
2073  }
2074  if (row_number == 0)
2075  {
2076  for (i = 0; i < row_array_size; ++i)
2077  {
2078  if (RowOperationPtr[i] == SQL_ROW_IGNORE)
2079  {
2080  continue;
2081  }
2082  rc = odbc_set_pos_update (stmt, &bookmark_desc_info, desc_info_ptr, i + 1);
2083  if (rc < 0)
2084  {
2085  error_flag = 1;
2086  RowStatusPtr[i] = SQL_ROW_ERROR;
2087  }
2088  else
2089  {
2090  RowStatusPtr[i] = SQL_ROW_UPDATED;
2091  }
2092  }
2093  }
2094  else
2095  {
2096  rc = odbc_set_pos_update (stmt, &bookmark_desc_info, desc_info_ptr, row_number);
2097  if (rc < 0)
2098  {
2099  error_flag = 1;
2100  RowStatusPtr[row_number - 1] = SQL_ROW_ERROR;
2101  }
2102  else
2103  {
2104  RowStatusPtr[row_number - 1] = SQL_ROW_UPDATED;
2105  }
2106  }
2107 
2108  NC_FREE (desc_info_ptr);
2109  break;
2110 
2111  case SQL_DELETE:
2112  if (row_number == 0)
2113  {
2114  for (i = 0; i < row_array_size; ++i)
2115  {
2116  if (RowOperationPtr[i] == SQL_ROW_IGNORE)
2117  {
2118  continue;
2119  }
2120  rc = odbc_set_pos_delete (stmt, &bookmark_desc_info, i + 1);
2121  if (rc < 0)
2122  {
2123  error_flag = 1;
2124  RowStatusPtr[i] = SQL_ROW_ERROR;
2125  }
2126  else
2127  {
2128  RowStatusPtr[i] = SQL_ROW_DELETED;
2129  }
2130  }
2131  }
2132  else
2133  {
2134  rc = odbc_set_pos_delete (stmt, &bookmark_desc_info, row_number);
2135  if (rc < 0)
2136  {
2137  error_flag = 1;
2138  RowStatusPtr[row_number - 1] = SQL_ROW_ERROR;
2139  }
2140  else
2141  {
2142  RowStatusPtr[row_number - 1] = SQL_ROW_DELETED;
2143  }
2144  }
2145  break;
2146  }
2147 
2148  if (error_flag == 1)
2149  return ODBC_ERROR;
2150 
2151  return ODBC_SUCCESS;
2152 }
2153 
2154 /************************************************************************
2155 * name: reset_result_set
2156 * arguments:
2157 * returns/side-effects:
2158 * description:
2159 * NOTE:
2160 * IRD는 SQLPrepare 시점에서 이루어지므로, 여기서 IRD를 delete해서는* 안된다. 왜냐면 SQLExecute도 reset_result_set을 사용하고, * SQLCloseCursor시 IRD가 delete되지 않기 때문이다. ************************************************************************/ PUBLIC void reset_result_set (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt) { if (stmt->result_type == NULL_RESULT) return; // delete catalog result set if (stmt->catalog_result.value != NULL) { free_catalog_result (stmt->catalog_result.value, stmt->result_type); stmt->catalog_result.value = NULL; stmt->catalog_result.current = NULL; } // reset result set state stmt->result_type = NULL_RESULT; stmt->data_at_exec_state = STMT_NEED_NO_MORE_DATA; stmt->tpl_number = 0; stmt->current_tpl_pos = 0; NA_FREE (stmt->cursor); // reset column data free_column_data (&stmt->column_data, RESET); } /************************************************************************ * name: create_ird * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PUBLIC void create_ird (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, T_CCI_COL_INFO * cci_col_info, int column_number) { T_CCI_U_TYPE cci_u_type; short col_type; int col_scale; int col_precision; short col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE_UNKNOWN; short col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_READONLY; char *table_name; char *col_name; short i; if (stmt == NULL || cci_col_info == NULL) return; if (cci_col_info != NULL) { if (GET_STAT_STMT_TYPE (stmt->stmt_type)) { col_type = SQL_VARCHAR; col_precision = MAX_CUBRID_CHAR_LEN; col_scale = 0; col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE_UNKNOWN; col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_READONLY; col_name = "GET_STAT"; odbc_set_ird (stmt, 1, col_type, "", col_name, col_precision, (short) col_scale, col_nullable, col_updatable); } else if (METHOD_STMT_TYPE (stmt->stmt_type)) { col_type = SQL_VARCHAR; col_precision = MAX_CUBRID_CHAR_LEN; col_scale = 0; col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE_UNKNOWN; col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_READONLY; col_name = "METHOD_RESULT"; odbc_set_ird (stmt, 1, col_type, "", col_name, col_precision, (short) col_scale, col_nullable, col_updatable); } else { // CUBRID_STMT_SELECT if (stmt->attr_use_bookmark == SQL_UB_VARIABLE) { create_bookmark_ird (stmt); } if (IS_UPDATABLE (stmt->attr_cursor_type)) { if (cci_is_updatable (stmt->stmthd)) { col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_WRITE; } else { col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_READONLY; stmt->attr_concurrency = SQL_CONCUR_READ_ONLY; stmt->attr_cursor_sensitivity = SQL_INSENSITIVE; stmt->attr_cursor_type = SQL_CURSOR_STATIC; } } for (i = 1; i <= (signed) column_number; ++i) { cci_u_type = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_TYPE (cci_col_info, i); // OBJECT는 string으로 bind되기 때문에 display를 위해서 precision을 // 32로 설정하였다. if (cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_OBJECT) { cci_u_type = CCI_U_TYPE_CHAR; col_precision = 32; col_scale = 0; } else if (CCI_IS_COLLECTION_TYPE (cci_u_type)) { /* XXX : deprecated cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_SET || cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_MULTISET || cci_u_type * == CCI_U_TYPE_SEQUENCE ) { */ cci_u_type = CCI_U_TYPE_STRING; col_precision = MAX_CUBRID_CHAR_LEN; col_scale = 0; } else { col_precision = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_PRECISION (cci_col_info, i); // revise col_precision col_precision = (col_precision < 0) ? DEFAULT_COL_PRECISION : col_precision; #ifdef DELPHI col_type = odbc_type_by_cci (cci_u_type, col_precision); #endif if (cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_STRING || cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_CHAR) { if (col_precision >= stmt->conn->max_string_length) col_precision = stmt->conn->max_string_length; } col_scale = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_SCALE (cci_col_info, i); } col_name = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_NAME (cci_col_info, i); table_name = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_CLASS_NAME (cci_col_info, i); if (CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_IS_NON_NULL (cci_col_info, i) == 0) { // nullable col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE; } else if (CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_IS_NON_NULL (cci_col_info, i) == 1) { col_nullable = SQL_NO_NULLS; } else { col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE_UNKNOWN; } #ifndef DELPHI col_type = odbc_type_by_cci (cci_u_type, col_precision); #endif odbc_set_ird (stmt, i, col_type, table_name, col_name, col_precision, (short) col_scale, col_nullable, col_updatable); } } } } /************************************************************************ * name: next_param_data_at_exec * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * * description: * APD에서 param_pos이후의 record에 대해서 indicator가 DATA_AT_EXEC 인 것을 * 찾는다. 찾으면 record number, else -1 * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE short next_param_data_at_exec (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, short param_pos) { ODBC_RECORD *record = NULL; int i; if (param_pos > stmt->apd->max_count) { return -1; } for (i = param_pos + 1; i <= stmt->apd->max_count; ++i) { record = find_record_from_desc (stmt->apd, i); if (record != NULL) { if (IND_IS_DATA_AT_EXEC (*(record->indicator_ptr))) { return i; } } } return -1; } PUBLIC void free_column_data (COLUMN_DATA * data, int option) { if (data == NULL) return; switch (option) { case INIT: case RESET: case FREE_MEMBER: data->current_pt = NULL; data->column_no = 0; data->remain_length = 0; data->prev_return_status = -1; break; case FREE_ALL: default: data->current_pt = NULL; data->column_no = 0; data->remain_length = 0; data->prev_return_status = -1; UT_FREE (data); break; } } /************************************************************************ * name: get_appl_desc_info * arguments: * col_index - parameter col index, starting from 1 * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void get_appl_desc_info (ODBC_DESC * desc, short col_index, DescInfo * desc_info_ptr) { if (desc == NULL || desc_info_ptr == NULL) return; memset (desc_info_ptr, 0, sizeof (DescInfo)); desc_info_ptr->bind_type = desc->bind_type; /* 0 means single or column wise, >0 means row wise */ if (desc->bind_offset_ptr == NULL) { desc_info_ptr->offset_size = 0; } else { desc_info_ptr->offset_size = *(desc->bind_offset_ptr); } if (desc_info_ptr == NULL) return; odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_CONCISE_TYPE, &(desc_info_ptr->type), 0, NULL); odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_DATA_PTR, &(desc_info_ptr->value_ptr), 0, NULL); odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_INDICATOR_PTR, &(desc_info_ptr->ind_ptr), 0, NULL); odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_OCTET_LENGTH, &(desc_info_ptr->length), 0, NULL); odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_PRECISION, &(desc_info_ptr->precision), 0, NULL); odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_SCALE, &(desc_info_ptr->scale), 0, NULL); odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_OCTET_LENGTH_PTR, &(desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr), 0, NULL); } /************************************************************************ * name: recalculate_bind_pointer * arguments: * row_index - array index, starting from 1 * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void recalculate_bind_pointer (DescInfo * desc_info_ptr, SQLSETPOSIROW row_index, UINT_PTR * value_addr, UINT_PTR * ind_addr, UINT_PTR * octet_len_addr) { long element_size; if (desc_info_ptr->value_ptr == NULL) { (void *) *value_addr = NULL; (long *) *ind_addr = NULL; if (octet_len_addr) { (long *) *octet_len_addr = NULL; } } else { if (desc_info_ptr->bind_type == SQL_PARAM_BIND_BY_COLUMN) { *value_addr = (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->value_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * (desc_info_ptr->length); *ind_addr = (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->ind_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * sizeof (long); if (octet_len_addr) { if (desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr) *octet_len_addr = (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * sizeof (long); else (long *) *octet_len_addr = NULL; } } else { element_size = desc_info_ptr->bind_type; *value_addr = (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->value_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * element_size; *ind_addr = (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->ind_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * element_size; if (octet_len_addr) { if (desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr) *octet_len_addr = (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * element_size; else (long *) *octet_len_addr = NULL; } } } } /************************************************************************ * name: reset_revised_sql * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void reset_revised_sql (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt) { if (stmt == NULL) return; NA_FREE (stmt->revised_sql.sql_text); NA_FREE (stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_pos); NA_FREE (stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_val); NA_FREE (stmt->revised_sql.org_param_pos); stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_num = 0; } /************************************************************************ * name: reset_revised_sql * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE int revised_param_pos (char *param_pos, int index) { int i; short rv; char *pt; char buf[128]; int revised_pos = 0; if (param_pos == NULL) return 0; pt = param_pos; i = 0; while ((rv = element_from_setstring (&pt, buf)) > 0) { ++i; if (i == index) { revised_pos = atoi (buf); break; } } return revised_pos; } /************************************************************************ * name: get_flag_of_cci_prepare * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * flag of cci_execute() * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE char get_flag_of_cci_prepare (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt) { if (stmt == NULL) return 0; if (IS_UPDATABLE (stmt->attr_cursor_type)) { return (CCI_PREPARE_UPDATABLE | CCI_PREPARE_INCLUDE_OID); } return 0; } /************************************************************************ * name: get_flag_of_cci_execute * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * flag of cci_execute() * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE char get_flag_of_cci_execute (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt) { if (stmt == NULL) return 0; return CCI_EXEC_QUERY_ALL; } /************************************************************************ * name: create_bookmark_ird * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * 0번 ird record는 BOOKMARK를 위한 것이다. * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void create_bookmark_ird (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt) { short verbose_type; long display_size; long octet_length; ODBC_RECORD *record; short type; long precision; short scale; if (stmt == NULL) return; record = find_record_from_desc (stmt->ird, 0); if (record == NULL) { odbc_alloc_record (stmt->ird, &record, 0); } type = SQL_VARBINARY; precision = 4; scale = 0; verbose_type = odbc_concise_to_verbose_type (type); display_size = odbc_display_size (type, precision); octet_length = odbc_octet_length (type, precision); odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_CONCISE_TYPE, (SQLPOINTER) type, 0, 1); odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_TYPE_NAME, (SQLPOINTER) odbc_type_name (type), SQL_NTS, 1); odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_TYPE, (SQLPOINTER) verbose_type, 0, 1); if (IS_STRING_TYPE (type) || IS_BINARY_TYPE (type)) { odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_PRECISION, (SQLPOINTER) 0, 0, 1); // precision에 대해서 정의하고 있지 않다. } else if (odbc_is_valid_sql_date_type (type)) { odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_PRECISION, (SQLPOINTER) 0, 0, 1); // CUBRID은 date type에 대해서 precision(for second)은 0이다. // date type에 대한 length는 char형색의 display size와 같다. } else { odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_PRECISION, (SQLPOINTER) precision, 0, 1); } odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_LENGTH, (SQLPOINTER) display_size, 0, 1); odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_OCTET_LENGTH, (SQLPOINTER) octet_length, 0, 1); odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_SCALE, (SQLPOINTER) scale, 0, 1); odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_DISPLAY_SIZE, (SQLPOINTER) display_size, 0, 1); odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_UNSIGNED, (SQLPOINTER) SQL_TRUE, 0, 1); } /************************************************************************ * name: make_param_array * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: * 이미 param_array에는 memory가 할당된 상태이다. ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void make_param_array (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, short column_index, DescInfo * desc_info, ParamArray * param_array, int array_size) { SQLSETPOSIROW h; unsigned long i; void *value_ptr; long *ind_ptr; void *cci_value = NULL; unsigned short *ParamOperationArrayPtr; odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_PARAM_OPERATION_PTR, &ParamOperationArrayPtr, 0, NULL); memory_alloc_param_array (param_array, array_size); for (h = 1, i = 0; h <= stmt->apd->array_size; ++h) { if (stmt->apd->array_size > 1) { if (ParamOperationArrayPtr != NULL && ParamOperationArrayPtr[h - 1] == SQL_PARAM_IGNORE) { continue; } } recalculate_bind_pointer (desc_info, h, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); if (ind_ptr != NULL && *ind_ptr == SQL_NULL_DATA) { param_array->ind_array[i] = 1; ((char **) param_array->value_array)[i] = NULL; } else { param_array->ind_array[i] = 0; odbc_value_to_cci2 (param_array->value_array, i, value_ptr, desc_info->type, desc_info->length, desc_info->precision, desc_info->scale); } ++i; } } /************************************************************************ * name: * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void memory_alloc_param_array (ParamArray * param_array, int array_size) { param_array->ind_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (int) * array_size); switch (param_array->value_type) { case CCI_A_TYPE_STR: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (char *) * array_size); break; case CCI_A_TYPE_BIGINT: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (__int64) * array_size); break; case CCI_A_TYPE_INT: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (int) * array_size); break; case CCI_A_TYPE_FLOAT: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (float) * array_size); break; case CCI_A_TYPE_DOUBLE: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (double) * array_size); break; case CCI_A_TYPE_BIT: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (T_CCI_BIT) * array_size); break; case CCI_A_TYPE_SET: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (T_CCI_SET) * array_size); break; case CCI_A_TYPE_DATE: param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (T_CCI_DATE) * array_size); break; } } /************************************************************************ * name: delete_row_by_cursor_pos * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE RETCODE delete_row_by_cursor_pos (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, unsigned long cursor_pos) { int cci_rc = 0; T_CCI_ERROR cci_err_buf; char oid_buf[32]; cci_rc = cci_cursor (stmt->stmthd, cursor_pos, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &cci_err_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error); cci_rc = cci_fetch (stmt->stmthd, &cci_err_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error); cci_rc = cci_get_cur_oid (stmt->stmthd, oid_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error); cci_rc = cci_oid (stmt->conn->connhd, CCI_OID_DROP, oid_buf, &cci_err_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error); return ODBC_SUCCESS; cci_error: if (cci_rc < 0) odbc_set_diag_by_cci (stmt->diag, cci_rc, &cci_err_buf); return ODBC_ERROR; } /************************************************************************ * name: odbc_set_pos_update * arguments: * row_pos - row position in ard. (starting from 1) * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE RETCODE odbc_set_pos_update (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, DescInfo * bookmark_desc_info_ptr, DescInfo * desc_info_ptr, SQLSETPOSIROW row_pos) { short max_col_num, j; void *value_ptr; long *ind_ptr; long bookmark; T_CCI_A_TYPE a_type; int cci_rc = 0; T_CCI_ERROR cci_err_buf; void *cci_value = NULL; if (stmt == NULL || bookmark_desc_info_ptr == NULL || desc_info_ptr == NULL) return ODBC_ERROR; max_col_num = stmt->ard->max_count; recalculate_bind_pointer (bookmark_desc_info_ptr, row_pos, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); bookmark = *((long *) value_ptr); for (j = 1; j <= stmt->ard->max_count; ++j) { recalculate_bind_pointer (&desc_info_ptr[j - 1], row_pos, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); a_type = odbc_type_to_cci_a_type (desc_info_ptr[j - 1].type); if (*ind_ptr == SQL_COLUMN_IGNORE) { continue; } else if (*ind_ptr == SQL_NULL_DATA) { cci_rc = cci_cursor_update (stmt->stmthd, bookmark, j, a_type, (void *) NULL, &cci_err_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error); } else { cci_value = odbc_value_to_cci (value_ptr, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].type, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].length, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].precision, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].scale); cci_rc = cci_cursor_update (stmt->stmthd, bookmark, j, a_type, value_ptr, &cci_err_buf); ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error); NA_FREE (cci_value); } } return ODBC_SUCCESS; cci_error: NA_FREE (cci_value); odbc_set_diag_by_cci (stmt->diag, cci_rc, &cci_err_buf); return ODBC_ERROR; } /************************************************************************ * name: odbc_set_pos_delete * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE RETCODE odbc_set_pos_delete (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, DescInfo * bookmark_desc_info_ptr, SQLSETPOSIROW row_pos) { RETCODE rc; void *value_ptr; long *ind_ptr; long bookmark; if (stmt == NULL) return ODBC_ERROR; recalculate_bind_pointer (bookmark_desc_info_ptr, row_pos, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL); bookmark = *((long *) value_ptr); rc = delete_row_by_cursor_pos (stmt, bookmark); if (rc < 0) return ODBC_ERROR; return ODBC_SUCCESS; } /************************************************************************ * name: free_param_array * arguments: * returns/side-effects: * description: * NOTE: ************************************************************************/ PRIVATE void free_param_array (ParamArray * param_ptr, int param_count, int array_count) { int i; int j; char **cpt; T_CCI_BIT *bpt; if (param_ptr == NULL || param_count < 0) return; for (i = 0; i < param_count; ++i) { switch (param_ptr[i].value_type) { case CCI_A_TYPE_STR: cpt = param_ptr[i].value_array; for (j = 0; j < array_count; ++j) { NC_FREE (cpt[j]); } break; case CCI_A_TYPE_BIT: bpt = param_ptr[i].value_array; for (j = 0; j < array_count; ++j) { NC_FREE (bpt[i].buf); } break; } NC_FREE (param_ptr[i].value_array); NC_FREE (param_ptr[i].ind_array); } free (param_ptr); } #ifdef _DEBUG PRIVATE void debug_print_appl_desc (DescInfo * desc_info, void *value_ptr, long *ind_ptr) { switch (desc_info->type) { case SQL_C_SHORT: // for 2.x backward compatibility case SQL_C_SSHORT: case SQL_C_USHORT: printf ("[short] %d ||", *(short *) value_ptr); break; case SQL_C_STINYINT: case SQL_C_UTINYINT: case SQL_C_TINYINT: // for 2.x backward compatibility printf ("[short] %d ||", *(char *) value_ptr); break; case SQL_C_LONG: // for 2.x backward compatibility case SQL_C_SLONG: case SQL_C_ULONG: printf ("[long] %ld || ", *(long *) value_ptr); break; case SQL_C_SBIGINT: case SQL_C_UBIGINT: printf ("[bigint] %lld || ", (long long) (*(__int64 *) value_ptr)); break; /*--------------------------------------------------------------- * floating point type *--------------------------------------------------------------*/ case SQL_C_FLOAT: printf ("[float] %f || ", *(float *) value_ptr); break; case SQL_C_DOUBLE: printf ("[double] %lf || ", *(double *) value_ptr); break; /*--------------------------------------------------------------- * char & binary type *--------------------------------------------------------------*/ case SQL_C_CHAR: printf ("[string] %s || ", (char *) value_ptr); break; } } #endif PRIVATE short default_type_to_c_type (short value_type, short parameter_type) { switch (parameter_type) { case SQL_CHAR: case SQL_VARCHAR: case SQL_LONGVARCHAR: return SQL_C_CHAR; case SQL_WCHAR: case SQL_WVARCHAR: case SQL_WLONGVARCHAR: return SQL_C_WCHAR; case SQL_DECIMAL: case SQL_NUMERIC: return SQL_C_CHAR; case SQL_BIT: return SQL_C_BIT; case SQL_TINYINT: return SQL_C_TINYINT; case SQL_SMALLINT: return SQL_C_SSHORT; case SQL_INTEGER: return SQL_C_SLONG; case SQL_BIGINT: return SQL_C_SBIGINT; case SQL_REAL: return SQL_C_FLOAT; case SQL_FLOAT: case SQL_DOUBLE: return SQL_C_DOUBLE; case SQL_BINARY: case SQL_VARBINARY: case SQL_LONGVARBINARY: return SQL_C_BINARY; case SQL_TYPE_DATE: return SQL_C_TYPE_DATE; case SQL_TYPE_TIME: return SQL_C_TYPE_TIME; case SQL_TYPE_TIMESTAMP: return SQL_C_TYPE_TIMESTAMP; case SQL_GUID: return SQL_C_CHAR; } return value_type; }
2161 * 안된다. 왜냐면 SQLExecute도 reset_result_set을 사용하고,
2162 * SQLCloseCursor시 IRD가 delete되지 않기 때문이다.
2163 ************************************************************************/
2164 PUBLIC void
2165 reset_result_set (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt)
2166 {
2167  if (stmt->result_type == NULL_RESULT)
2168  return;
2169 
2170  // delete catalog result set
2171  if (stmt->catalog_result.value != NULL)
2172  {
2173  free_catalog_result (stmt->catalog_result.value, stmt->result_type);
2174  stmt->catalog_result.value = NULL;
2175  stmt->catalog_result.current = NULL;
2176  }
2177 
2178  // reset result set state
2179  stmt->result_type = NULL_RESULT;
2180  stmt->data_at_exec_state = STMT_NEED_NO_MORE_DATA;
2181  stmt->tpl_number = 0;
2182  stmt->current_tpl_pos = 0;
2183  NA_FREE (stmt->cursor);
2184 
2185  // reset column data
2186  free_column_data (&stmt->column_data, RESET);
2187 }

2189 /************************************************************************
2190 * name: create_ird
2191 * arguments:
2192 * returns/side-effects:
2193 * description:
2194 * NOTE:
2195 ************************************************************************/
2196 PUBLIC void
2197 create_ird (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, T_CCI_COL_INFO * cci_col_info, int column_number)
2198 {
2199  T_CCI_U_TYPE cci_u_type;
2200  short col_type;
2201  int col_scale;
2202  int col_precision;
2203  short col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE_UNKNOWN;
2204  short col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_READONLY;
2205  char *table_name;
2206  char *col_name;
2207  short i;
2208 
2209  if (stmt == NULL || cci_col_info == NULL)
2210  return;
2211 
2212  if (cci_col_info != NULL)
2213  {
2214 
2215  if (GET_STAT_STMT_TYPE (stmt->stmt_type))
2216  {
2217  col_type = SQL_VARCHAR;
2218  col_precision = MAX_CUBRID_CHAR_LEN;
2219  col_scale = 0;
2220  col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE_UNKNOWN;
2221  col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_READONLY;
2222  col_name = "GET_STAT";
2223  odbc_set_ird (stmt, 1, col_type, "", col_name, col_precision, (short) col_scale, col_nullable, col_updatable);
2224  }
2225  else if (METHOD_STMT_TYPE (stmt->stmt_type))
2226  {
2227  col_type = SQL_VARCHAR;
2228  col_precision = MAX_CUBRID_CHAR_LEN;
2229  col_scale = 0;
2230  col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE_UNKNOWN;
2231  col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_READONLY;
2232  col_name = "METHOD_RESULT";
2233  odbc_set_ird (stmt, 1, col_type, "", col_name, col_precision, (short) col_scale, col_nullable, col_updatable);
2234  }
2235  else
2236  {
2237  // CUBRID_STMT_SELECT
2238 
2239  if (stmt->attr_use_bookmark == SQL_UB_VARIABLE)
2240  {
2241  create_bookmark_ird (stmt);
2242  }
2243 
2244  if (IS_UPDATABLE (stmt->attr_cursor_type))
2245  {
2246  if (cci_is_updatable (stmt->stmthd))
2247  {
2248  col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_WRITE;
2249  }
2250  else
2251  {
2252  col_updatable = SQL_ATTR_READONLY;
2253  stmt->attr_concurrency = SQL_CONCUR_READ_ONLY;
2254  stmt->attr_cursor_sensitivity = SQL_INSENSITIVE;
2255  stmt->attr_cursor_type = SQL_CURSOR_STATIC;
2256  }
2257  }
2258 
2259  for (i = 1; i <= (signed) column_number; ++i)
2260  {
2261 
2262  cci_u_type = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_TYPE (cci_col_info, i);
2263 
2264  // OBJECT는 string으로 bind되기 때문에 display를 위해서 precision을
2265  // 32로 설정하였다.
2266 
2267  if (cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_OBJECT)
2268  {
2269  cci_u_type = CCI_U_TYPE_CHAR;
2270  col_precision = 32;
2271  col_scale = 0;
2272  }
2273  else if (CCI_IS_COLLECTION_TYPE (cci_u_type))
2274  {
2275  /* XXX : deprecated cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_SET || cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_MULTISET || cci_u_type
2276  * == CCI_U_TYPE_SEQUENCE ) { */
2277  cci_u_type = CCI_U_TYPE_STRING;
2278  col_precision = MAX_CUBRID_CHAR_LEN;
2279  col_scale = 0;
2280  }
2281  else
2282  {
2283  col_precision = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_PRECISION (cci_col_info, i);
2284  // revise col_precision
2285  col_precision = (col_precision < 0) ? DEFAULT_COL_PRECISION : col_precision;
2286 #ifdef DELPHI
2287  col_type = odbc_type_by_cci (cci_u_type, col_precision);
2288 #endif
2289  if (cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_STRING || cci_u_type == CCI_U_TYPE_CHAR)
2290  {
2291  if (col_precision >= stmt->conn->max_string_length)
2292  col_precision = stmt->conn->max_string_length;
2293  }
2294  col_scale = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_SCALE (cci_col_info, i);
2295  }
2296 
2297  col_name = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_NAME (cci_col_info, i);
2298  table_name = CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_CLASS_NAME (cci_col_info, i);
2299 
2300  if (CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_IS_NON_NULL (cci_col_info, i) == 0)
2301  { // nullable
2302  col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE;
2303  }
2304  else if (CCI_GET_RESULT_INFO_IS_NON_NULL (cci_col_info, i) == 1)
2305  {
2306  col_nullable = SQL_NO_NULLS;
2307  }
2308  else
2309  {
2310  col_nullable = SQL_NULLABLE_UNKNOWN;
2311  }
2312 #ifndef DELPHI
2313  col_type = odbc_type_by_cci (cci_u_type, col_precision);
2314 #endif
2315 
2316  odbc_set_ird (stmt, i, col_type, table_name, col_name, col_precision, (short) col_scale, col_nullable,
2317  col_updatable);
2318 
2319  }
2320  }
2321  }
2322 }
2323 
2324 /************************************************************************
2325 * name: next_param_data_at_exec
2326 * arguments:
2327 * returns/side-effects:
2328 *
2329 * description:
2330 * APD에서 param_pos이후의 record에 대해서 indicator가 DATA_AT_EXEC 인 것을
2331 * 찾는다. 찾으면 record number, else -1
2332 * NOTE:
2333 ************************************************************************/
2334 PRIVATE short
2335 next_param_data_at_exec (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, short param_pos)
2336 {
2337  ODBC_RECORD *record = NULL;
2338  int i;
2339 
2340 
2341  if (param_pos > stmt->apd->max_count)
2342  {
2343  return -1;
2344  }
2345 
2346  for (i = param_pos + 1; i <= stmt->apd->max_count; ++i)
2347  {
2348  record = find_record_from_desc (stmt->apd, i);
2349  if (record != NULL)
2350  {
2351  if (IND_IS_DATA_AT_EXEC (*(record->indicator_ptr)))
2352  {
2353  return i;
2354  }
2355  }
2356  }
2357 
2358  return -1;
2359 }
2360 
2361 PUBLIC void
2362 free_column_data (COLUMN_DATA * data, int option)
2363 {
2364  if (data == NULL)
2365  return;
2366 
2367  switch (option)
2368  {
2369  case INIT:
2370  case RESET:
2371  case FREE_MEMBER:
2372  data->current_pt = NULL;
2373  data->column_no = 0;
2374  data->remain_length = 0;
2375  data->prev_return_status = -1;
2376  break;
2377 
2378  case FREE_ALL:
2379  default:
2380  data->current_pt = NULL;
2381  data->column_no = 0;
2382  data->remain_length = 0;
2383  data->prev_return_status = -1;
2384  UT_FREE (data);
2385 
2386  break;
2387  }
2388 }

2391 /************************************************************************
2392 * name: get_appl_desc_info
2393 * arguments:
2394 
2395 * col_index - parameter col index, starting from 1
2396 * returns/side-effects:
2397 * description:
2398 * NOTE:
2399 ************************************************************************/
2400 PRIVATE void
2401 get_appl_desc_info (ODBC_DESC * desc, short col_index, DescInfo * desc_info_ptr)
2402 {
2403  if (desc == NULL || desc_info_ptr == NULL)
2404  return;
2405 
2406  memset (desc_info_ptr, 0, sizeof (DescInfo));
2407 
2408 
2409  desc_info_ptr->bind_type = desc->bind_type;
2410  /* 0 means single or column wise, >0 means row wise */
2411  if (desc->bind_offset_ptr == NULL)
2412  {
2413  desc_info_ptr->offset_size = 0;
2414  }
2415  else
2416  {
2417  desc_info_ptr->offset_size = *(desc->bind_offset_ptr);
2418  }
2419 
2420  if (desc_info_ptr == NULL)
2421  return;
2422 
2423  odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_CONCISE_TYPE, &(desc_info_ptr->type), 0, NULL);
2424  odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_DATA_PTR, &(desc_info_ptr->value_ptr), 0, NULL);
2425  odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_INDICATOR_PTR, &(desc_info_ptr->ind_ptr), 0, NULL);
2426  odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_OCTET_LENGTH, &(desc_info_ptr->length), 0, NULL);
2427  odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_PRECISION, &(desc_info_ptr->precision), 0, NULL);
2428  odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_SCALE, &(desc_info_ptr->scale), 0, NULL);
2429  odbc_get_desc_field (desc, col_index, SQL_DESC_OCTET_LENGTH_PTR, &(desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr), 0, NULL);
2430 }
2431 
2432 /************************************************************************
2433 * name: recalculate_bind_pointer
2434 * arguments:
2435 * row_index - array index, starting from 1
2436 * returns/side-effects:
2437 * description:
2438 * NOTE:
2439 ************************************************************************/
2440 PRIVATE void
2441 recalculate_bind_pointer (DescInfo * desc_info_ptr, SQLSETPOSIROW row_index, UINT_PTR * value_addr, UINT_PTR * ind_addr,
2442  UINT_PTR * octet_len_addr)
2443 {
2444  long element_size;
2445 
2446  if (desc_info_ptr->value_ptr == NULL)
2447  {
2448  (void *) *value_addr = NULL;
2449  (long *) *ind_addr = NULL;
2450  if (octet_len_addr)
2451  {
2452  (long *) *octet_len_addr = NULL;
2453  }
2454  }
2455  else
2456  {
2457  if (desc_info_ptr->bind_type == SQL_PARAM_BIND_BY_COLUMN)
2458  {
2459  *value_addr =
2460  (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->value_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index -
2461  1) * (desc_info_ptr->length);
2462  *ind_addr = (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->ind_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * sizeof (long);
2463  if (octet_len_addr)
2464  {
2465  if (desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr)
2466  *octet_len_addr =
2467  (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index -
2468  1) * sizeof (long);
2469  else
2470  (long *) *octet_len_addr = NULL;
2471  }
2472  }
2473  else
2474  {
2475  element_size = desc_info_ptr->bind_type;
2476  *value_addr =
2477  (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->value_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * element_size;
2478  *ind_addr = (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->ind_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * element_size;
2479  if (octet_len_addr)
2480  {
2481  if (desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr)
2482  *octet_len_addr =
2483  (UINT_PTR) desc_info_ptr->octet_len_ptr + desc_info_ptr->offset_size + (row_index - 1) * element_size;
2484  else
2485  (long *) *octet_len_addr = NULL;
2486  }
2487  }
2488  }
2489 }

2491 /************************************************************************
2492  * name: reset_revised_sql

2494  * returns/side-effects:
2495  * description:

2498 PRIVATE void
2499 reset_revised_sql (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt)

2502  return;
2503 
2504  NA_FREE (stmt->revised_sql.sql_text);
2505  NA_FREE (stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_pos);
2506  NA_FREE (stmt->revised_sql.oid_param_val);

2508

2510

2513 /************************************************************************
2514  * name: reset_revised_sql
2515  * arguments:
2516  * returns/side-effects:
2517  * description:
2518  * NOTE:
2519  ************************************************************************/
2520 PRIVATE int
2521 revised_param_pos (char *param_pos, int index)
2522 {
2523  int i;
2524  short rv;
2525  char *pt;
2526  char buf[128];
2527  int revised_pos = 0;
2528 
2529  if (param_pos == NULL)
2530  return 0;
2531 
2532  pt = param_pos;
2533  i = 0;
2534 
2535  while ((rv = element_from_setstring (&pt, buf)) > 0)
2536  {
2537  ++i;
2538  if (i == index)
2539  {
2540  revised_pos = atoi (buf);
2541  break;
2542  }
2543  }
2544 
2545  return revised_pos;
2546 
2547 }

2588 /************************************************************************
2589  * name: create_bookmark_ird
2590  * arguments:
2591  * returns/side-effects:
2592  * description:
2593  * 0번 ird record는 BOOKMARK를 위한 것이다.
2594  * NOTE:
2595  ************************************************************************/
2596 PRIVATE void
2597 create_bookmark_ird (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt)
2598 {
2599  short verbose_type;
2600  long display_size;
2601  long octet_length;
2602  ODBC_RECORD *record;
2603  short type;
2604  long precision;
2605  short scale;
2606 
2607  if (stmt == NULL)
2608  return;
2609 
2610  record = find_record_from_desc (stmt->ird, 0);
2611  if (record == NULL)
2612  {
2613  odbc_alloc_record (stmt->ird, &record, 0);
2614  }
2615 
2616  type = SQL_VARBINARY;
2617  precision = 4;
2618  scale = 0;
2619  verbose_type = odbc_concise_to_verbose_type (type);
2620  display_size = odbc_display_size (type, precision);
2621  octet_length = odbc_octet_length (type, precision);
2622 
2623  odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_CONCISE_TYPE, (SQLPOINTER) type, 0, 1);
2624  odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_TYPE_NAME, (SQLPOINTER) odbc_type_name (type), SQL_NTS, 1);
2625  odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_TYPE, (SQLPOINTER) verbose_type, 0, 1);
2626  if (IS_STRING_TYPE (type) || IS_BINARY_TYPE (type))
2627  {
2628  odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_PRECISION, (SQLPOINTER) 0, 0, 1);
2629  // precision에 대해서 정의하고 있지 않다.
2630  }
2631  else if (odbc_is_valid_sql_date_type (type))
2632  {
2633  odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_PRECISION, (SQLPOINTER) 0, 0, 1);
2634  // CUBRID은 date type에 대해서 precision(for second)은 0이다.
2635  // date type에 대한 length는 char형색의 display size와 같다.
2636  }
2637  else
2638  {
2639  odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_PRECISION, (SQLPOINTER) precision, 0, 1);
2640  }
2641  odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_LENGTH, (SQLPOINTER) display_size, 0, 1);
2642  odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_OCTET_LENGTH, (SQLPOINTER) octet_length, 0, 1);
2643  odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_SCALE, (SQLPOINTER) scale, 0, 1);
2644  odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_DISPLAY_SIZE, (SQLPOINTER) display_size, 0, 1);
2645  odbc_set_desc_field (stmt->ird, 0, SQL_DESC_UNSIGNED, (SQLPOINTER) SQL_TRUE, 0, 1);
2646 
2647 }
2648 
2649 /************************************************************************
2650  * name: make_param_array
2651  * arguments:
2652  * returns/side-effects:
2653  * description:
2654  * NOTE:
2655  * 이미 param_array에는 memory가 할당된 상태이다.
2656  ************************************************************************/
2657 PRIVATE void
2658 make_param_array (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, short column_index, DescInfo * desc_info, ParamArray * param_array,
2659  int array_size)
2660 {
2661  SQLSETPOSIROW h;
2662  unsigned long i;
2663  void *value_ptr;
2664  long *ind_ptr;
2665  void *cci_value = NULL;
2666  unsigned short *ParamOperationArrayPtr;
2667 
2668  odbc_get_stmt_attr (stmt, SQL_ATTR_PARAM_OPERATION_PTR, &ParamOperationArrayPtr, 0, NULL);
2669 
2670  memory_alloc_param_array (param_array, array_size);
2671 
2672  for (h = 1, i = 0; h <= stmt->apd->array_size; ++h)
2673  {
2674  if (stmt->apd->array_size > 1)
2675  {
2676  if (ParamOperationArrayPtr != NULL && ParamOperationArrayPtr[h - 1] == SQL_PARAM_IGNORE)
2677  {
2678  continue;
2679  }
2680  }
2681 
2682  recalculate_bind_pointer (desc_info, h, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL);
2683 
2684  if (ind_ptr != NULL && *ind_ptr == SQL_NULL_DATA)
2685  {
2686  param_array->ind_array[i] = 1;
2687  ((char **) param_array->value_array)[i] = NULL;
2688  }
2689  else
2690  {
2691  param_array->ind_array[i] = 0;
2692  odbc_value_to_cci2 (param_array->value_array, i, value_ptr, desc_info->type, desc_info->length,
2693  desc_info->precision, desc_info->scale);
2694  }
2695  ++i;
2696  }
2697 
2698 }
2699 
2700 /************************************************************************
2701  * name:
2702  * arguments:
2703  * returns/side-effects:
2704  * description:
2705  * NOTE:
2706  ************************************************************************/
2707 PRIVATE void
2708 memory_alloc_param_array (ParamArray * param_array, int array_size)
2709 {
2710  param_array->ind_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (int) * array_size);
2711 
2712  switch (param_array->value_type)
2713  {
2714  case CCI_A_TYPE_STR:
2715  param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (char *) * array_size);
2716  break;
2717  case CCI_A_TYPE_BIGINT:
2718  param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (__int64) * array_size);
2719  break;
2720  case CCI_A_TYPE_INT:
2721  param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (int) * array_size);
2722  break;
2723  case CCI_A_TYPE_FLOAT:
2724  param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (float) * array_size);
2725  break;
2726  case CCI_A_TYPE_DOUBLE:
2727  param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (double) * array_size);
2728  break;
2729  case CCI_A_TYPE_BIT:
2730  param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (T_CCI_BIT) * array_size);
2731  break;
2732  case CCI_A_TYPE_SET:
2733  param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (T_CCI_SET) * array_size);
2734  break;
2735  case CCI_A_TYPE_DATE:
2736  param_array->value_array = UT_ALLOC (sizeof (T_CCI_DATE) * array_size);
2737  break;
2738  }
2739 
2740 }
2741 
2742 /************************************************************************
2743  * name: delete_row_by_cursor_pos
2744  * arguments:
2745  * returns/side-effects:
2746  * description:
2747  * NOTE:
2748  ************************************************************************/
2749 PRIVATE RETCODE
2750 delete_row_by_cursor_pos (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, unsigned long cursor_pos)
2751 {
2752  int cci_rc = 0;
2753  T_CCI_ERROR cci_err_buf;
2754  char oid_buf[32];
2755 
2756  cci_rc = cci_cursor (stmt->stmthd, cursor_pos, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &cci_err_buf);
2757  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
2758 
2759  cci_rc = cci_fetch (stmt->stmthd, &cci_err_buf);
2760  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
2761 
2762  cci_rc = cci_get_cur_oid (stmt->stmthd, oid_buf);
2763  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
2764 
2765  cci_rc = cci_oid (stmt->conn->connhd, CCI_OID_DROP, oid_buf, &cci_err_buf);
2766  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
2767 
2768  return ODBC_SUCCESS;
2769 
2770 cci_error:
2771  if (cci_rc < 0)
2772  odbc_set_diag_by_cci (stmt->diag, cci_rc, &cci_err_buf);
2773  return ODBC_ERROR;
2774 }
2775 
2776 
2777 /************************************************************************
2778  * name: odbc_set_pos_update
2779  * arguments:
2780  * row_pos - row position in ard. (starting from 1)
2781  * returns/side-effects:
2782  * description:
2783  * NOTE:
2784  ************************************************************************/
2785 PRIVATE RETCODE
2786 odbc_set_pos_update (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, DescInfo * bookmark_desc_info_ptr, DescInfo * desc_info_ptr,
2787  SQLSETPOSIROW row_pos)
2788 {
2789 
2790  short max_col_num, j;
2791  void *value_ptr;
2792  long *ind_ptr;
2793  long bookmark;
2794  T_CCI_A_TYPE a_type;
2795  int cci_rc = 0;
2796  T_CCI_ERROR cci_err_buf;
2797  void *cci_value = NULL;
2798 
2799  if (stmt == NULL || bookmark_desc_info_ptr == NULL || desc_info_ptr == NULL)
2800  return ODBC_ERROR;
2801 
2802  max_col_num = stmt->ard->max_count;
2803 
2804  recalculate_bind_pointer (bookmark_desc_info_ptr, row_pos, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL);
2805  bookmark = *((long *) value_ptr);
2806 
2807  for (j = 1; j <= stmt->ard->max_count; ++j)
2808  {
2809  recalculate_bind_pointer (&desc_info_ptr[j - 1], row_pos, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL);
2810  a_type = odbc_type_to_cci_a_type (desc_info_ptr[j - 1].type);
2811 
2812  if (*ind_ptr == SQL_COLUMN_IGNORE)
2813  {
2814  continue;
2815  }
2816  else if (*ind_ptr == SQL_NULL_DATA)
2817  {
2818  cci_rc = cci_cursor_update (stmt->stmthd, bookmark, j, a_type, (void *) NULL, &cci_err_buf);
2819  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
2820  }
2821  else
2822  {
2823  cci_value =
2824  odbc_value_to_cci (value_ptr, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].type, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].length,
2825  desc_info_ptr[j - 1].precision, desc_info_ptr[j - 1].scale);
2826 
2827  cci_rc = cci_cursor_update (stmt->stmthd, bookmark, j, a_type, value_ptr, &cci_err_buf);
2828  ERROR_GOTO (cci_rc, cci_error);
2829 
2830  NA_FREE (cci_value);
2831 
2832  }
2833  }
2834 
2835  return ODBC_SUCCESS;
2836 
2837 cci_error:
2838  NA_FREE (cci_value);
2839  odbc_set_diag_by_cci (stmt->diag, cci_rc, &cci_err_buf);
2840  return ODBC_ERROR;
2841 }
2842 
2843 
2844 /************************************************************************
2845  * name: odbc_set_pos_delete
2846  * arguments:
2847  * returns/side-effects:
2848  * description:
2849  * NOTE:
2850  ************************************************************************/
2851 PRIVATE RETCODE
2852 odbc_set_pos_delete (ODBC_STATEMENT * stmt, DescInfo * bookmark_desc_info_ptr, SQLSETPOSIROW row_pos)
2853 {
2854  RETCODE rc;
2855  void *value_ptr;
2856  long *ind_ptr;
2857  long bookmark;
2858 
2859  if (stmt == NULL)
2860  return ODBC_ERROR;
2861 
2862  recalculate_bind_pointer (bookmark_desc_info_ptr, row_pos, (UINT_PTR *) & value_ptr, (UINT_PTR *) & ind_ptr, NULL);
2863  bookmark = *((long *) value_ptr);
2864 
2865  rc = delete_row_by_cursor_pos (stmt, bookmark);
2866  if (rc < 0)
2867  return ODBC_ERROR;
2868 
2869  return ODBC_SUCCESS;
2870 }

2872 /************************************************************************
2873  * name: free_param_array
2874  * arguments:
2875  * returns/side-effects:
2876  * description:
2877  * NOTE:
2878  ************************************************************************/
2879 PRIVATE void
2880 free_param_array (ParamArray * param_ptr, int param_count, int array_count)
2881 {
2882  int i;
2883  int j;
2884  char **cpt;
2885  T_CCI_BIT *bpt;
2886 
2887  if (param_ptr == NULL || param_count < 0)
2888  return;
2889 
2890  for (i = 0; i < param_count; ++i)
2891  {
2892  switch (param_ptr[i].value_type)
2893  {
2894  case CCI_A_TYPE_STR:
2895  cpt = param_ptr[i].value_array;
2896  for (j = 0; j < array_count; ++j)
2897  {
2898  NC_FREE (cpt[j]);
2899  }
2900  break;
2901 
2902  case CCI_A_TYPE_BIT:
2903  bpt = param_ptr[i].value_array;
2904  for (j = 0; j < array_count; ++j)
2905  {
2906  NC_FREE (bpt[i].buf);
2907  }
2908  break;
2909 
2910  }
2911 
2912  NC_FREE (param_ptr[i].value_array);
2913  NC_FREE (param_ptr[i].ind_array);
2914  }
2915 
2916 
2917  free (param_ptr);
2918 }

2921 #ifdef _DEBUG
2922 PRIVATE void
2923 debug_print_appl_desc (DescInfo * desc_info, void *value_ptr, long *ind_ptr)
2924 {
2925  switch (desc_info->type)
2926  {
2927  case SQL_C_SHORT: // for 2.x backward compatibility
2928  case SQL_C_SSHORT:
2929  case SQL_C_USHORT:
2930  printf ("[short] %d ||", *(short *) value_ptr);
2931  break;
2932 
2933  case SQL_C_STINYINT:
2934  case SQL_C_UTINYINT:
2935  case SQL_C_TINYINT: // for 2.x backward compatibility
2936  printf ("[short] %d ||", *(char *) value_ptr);
2937  break;
2938 
2939  case SQL_C_LONG: // for 2.x backward compatibility
2940  case SQL_C_SLONG:
2941  case SQL_C_ULONG:
2942  printf ("[long] %ld || ", *(long *) value_ptr);
2943  break;
2944  case SQL_C_SBIGINT:
2945  case SQL_C_UBIGINT:
2946  printf ("[bigint] %lld || ", (long long) (*(__int64 *) value_ptr));
2947  break;
2948 
2949  /*---------------------------------------------------------------
2950  * floating point type
2951  *--------------------------------------------------------------*/
2952  case SQL_C_FLOAT:
2953  printf ("[float] %f || ", *(float *) value_ptr);
2954  break;
2955 
2956  case SQL_C_DOUBLE:
2957  printf ("[double] %lf || ", *(double *) value_ptr);
2958  break;
2959 
2960  /*---------------------------------------------------------------
2961  * char & binary type
2962  *--------------------------------------------------------------*/
2963  case SQL_C_CHAR:
2964  printf ("[string] %s || ", (char *) value_ptr);
2965  break;
2966  }
2967 }
2968 
2969 #endif

2971 PRIVATE short
2972 default_type_to_c_type (short value_type, short parameter_type)
2973 {
2974  switch (parameter_type)
2975  {
2976  case SQL_CHAR:
2977  case SQL_VARCHAR:
2978  case SQL_LONGVARCHAR:
2979  return SQL_C_CHAR;
2980  case SQL_WCHAR:
2981  case SQL_WVARCHAR:
2982  case SQL_WLONGVARCHAR:
2983  return SQL_C_WCHAR;
2984  case SQL_DECIMAL:
2985  case SQL_NUMERIC:
2986  return SQL_C_CHAR;
2987  case SQL_BIT:
2988  return SQL_C_BIT;
2989  case SQL_TINYINT:
2990  return SQL_C_TINYINT;
2991  case SQL_SMALLINT:
2992  return SQL_C_SSHORT;
2993  case SQL_INTEGER:
2994  return SQL_C_SLONG;
2995  case SQL_BIGINT:
2996  return SQL_C_SBIGINT;
2997  case SQL_REAL:
2998  return SQL_C_FLOAT;
2999  case SQL_FLOAT:
3000  case SQL_DOUBLE:
3001  return SQL_C_DOUBLE;
3002  case SQL_BINARY:
3003  case SQL_VARBINARY:
3004  case SQL_LONGVARBINARY:
3005  return SQL_C_BINARY;
3006  case SQL_TYPE_DATE:
3007  return SQL_C_TYPE_DATE;
3008  case SQL_TYPE_TIME:
3009  return SQL_C_TYPE_TIME;
3010  case SQL_TYPE_TIMESTAMP:
3011  return SQL_C_TYPE_TIMESTAMP;
3012  case SQL_GUID:
3013  return SQL_C_CHAR;
3014  }
3015  return value_type;
3016 }
